    this.Keystroke = function (shipmentRequest, vm, event) {
        debugger;
    }

// Source: Carrier Misroute (CMR) (CMR)_Client Business Rules_2487.cs
// shipping() // returns undefined
function shipping () {
            vm.shipping = {
                panelMessage: '',
                loadValue: '[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]',
                notificationInterval: 1800000, //30 minutes
                // notificationInterval: 1200000, //20 minutes
                // notificationInterval: 5000, //5 seconds
                videoModal: {
                    selector: '#VideoModalId',
                    zoom: {
                        in: zoomIn,
                        out: zoomOut,
                    },
                    close: videoModalClose,
                    stream: {
                        selector: '#CameraStreamId',
                        start: videoStreamStart,
                        stop: videoStreamStop,
                        captureImage: captureImage
                    }
                },
                imageFile: {
                    selector: '#CarrierLabelImageId',
                    upload: uploadCarrierLabelFile
                },
                menu: {
                    guide: {
                        inputFile: {
                            selector: '#inputFileDownload',
                        }
                    }
                },
                load: loadShip,
                customerChange: customerChange,
                getNotification: getNotification,
                selectDownloadFile: selectDownloadFile
            }
            vm.shipping.videoModal.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.imageFile.id = vm.shipping.imageFile.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.id = vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector.substring(1);

            $(document).on('change', vm.shipping.imageFile.selector, uploadCarrierLabelFile);
            $(document).on('change', vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector, inputFileDownloadChange);

            vm.shipping.slic = vm.UserInformation.SiteId ? vm.profile.Name.substring(0,5) : vm.profile.Name == thinClient.adminProfileName ? "XXXXX" : null;
            vm.shipping.customers = getShipperCustomers(vm.profile.Shippers);
            var enabledCustomers = vm.shipping.customers.filter(function(c) { return c.disabled != true; });
            vm.shipping.customer = enabledCustomers.length == 1 ? vm.shipping.customers[1] : vm.shipping.customers[0];
            vm.shipping.activePanel = vm.shipping.slic == undefined || vm.clientContext.Machine.Name == undefined ? 0 : 1;

            debugger;

            vm.fieldOptions = {
                Consignee: {
                    hideSaveAddress: true,
                    hideAddressSearch: true,
                    hideValidateAddress: true
                },
                ReturnAddress: {
                    hideSaveAddress: true,
                    hideAddressSearch: true,
                    hideValidateAddress: true
                }
            };
            vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference18.IsDisabled = true;
            vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference20.DefaultValue = vm.shipping.slic;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = vm.shipping.slic;

            activate();

            function activate() {
                if (!vm.profile.FieldOptions?.Reference?.IsHidden)
                    'form[name="referenceForm"] .panel > div'.unwrap();

                'name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] div[active="activeSubtabIndex"]'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[ng-hide="poBox.isHidden()"'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[active="activeSubtabIndex"]'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[ng-hide="residential.isHidden()"'.remove();


                vm.shipping.getNotification();
                thinClient.notificationIntervalId = setInterval(function() {
                    vm.shipping.getNotification();
                }, vm.shipping.notificationInterval);

                if (vm.shipping.customer.disabled)
                    vm.shipping.customer.selector.focus();
                else
                    vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
            }

            function getNotification() {
                var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id }
                thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                    if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications)) {
                        if (vm.clientContext.Site.Name == undefined)
                            vm.notification = null;
                        else {
                            var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id, SiteId: vm.clientContext.Site.Id };
                            thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                                if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications))
                                    vm.notification = null;

                                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                            })
                        }
                    }
                    vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                })

                this.setNotification = function(notifications) {
                    var notification = notifications.at(-1);
                    if (notification == undefined) return false;

                    this.notification = {
                        Title: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Title),
                        Message: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Message)
                    }
                    return true;
                }
            }

            function selectDownloadFile(event) {
                this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile = event.target.innerText;
                if (this.menu.guide.inputFile.selected) {
                    if (this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile.slice(-3) == this.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.name.slice(-3))
                        updateFile();
                } else {
                    var payload = { Action: 'downloadFile', Data: this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile };
                    var data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                    thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                        if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                            var data = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));

                            let linkData = `data:${data.fileType};base64,${data.encodedFile}`;
                            let downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
                            downloadLink.style.display = "none";
                            downloadLink.download = data.fileName;
                            downloadLink.href = linkData;
                            document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                            downloadLink.click();
                            document.body.removeChild(downloadLink);
                        }
                    });
                }

                function updateFile() {
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.onload = function () {
                        var request = {
                            Key: vm.shipping.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile,
                            Value: JSON.stringify({
                                fileType: vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.type,
                                fileName: vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.name,
                                encodedFile: this.result.split(',')[1]
                            })
                        }
                        var payload = { Action: 'updateFile', Data: request };
                        var data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                        thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                            if (ret.ErrorCode !== 0)
                                vm.notificationService.notifyDanger(ret.ErrorCode + " - " + ret.ErrorMessage);
                        }).catch(function (response) {
                            vm.notificationService.notifyDanger(vm.translations.Common.ErrorConnectingWCFService + ": " + response.status + " " + response.statusText);
                        })
                        vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected = null;
                        $(vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector).val(null);
                        vm.thinClient.loadData.show();

                    }
                    if (vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected) reader.readAsDataURL(vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected);
                }
            }

            function inputFileDownloadChange(event) {
                if (event.target.files == undefined) return;
                vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected = event.target.files[0];
                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
            }

            function getShipperCustomers(shippers) {
                var shipper = shippers.find(shipper => shipper.Symbol == vm.shipping.slic);
                if (shipper == undefined)
                     return [{ name: '--- No Shipper Configured ---', disabled: true }];

                var customData = shipper.CustomData.filter(c => c.Key.toUpperCase() == "CUSTOMER");
                var customers = customData.map(function(c) {
                    var customer = c.Value.toUpperCase();

                    if (customer == 'AMAZON')
                        return { name: "Amazon", value: customer, hasLoad: true, hasReturn: true, autoShip: true };
                    else if (customer == 'UPS')
                        return { name: "UPS", value: customer, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'DEMO')
                        return { name: "Demo", value: customer, hasLoad: false, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: false, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'FANATICS')
                        return { name: "Fanatics", value: customer, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else
                        return { name: `--- ${customer} ---`, disabled: true };
                });

                customers.sort(function(a, b) {
                    if (a.disabled && !b.disabled) return 1;
                    if (!a.disabled && b.disabled) return -1;
                    return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                });
                return [{ name: '--- Select Customer Option ---', selector: 'select[ng-model="vm.shipping.customer"]', disabled: true }].concat(customers);
            }

            function customerChange() {
                vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = vm.shipping.customer.value;
            }


            function videoModalClose () {

                if ($videoModal.is(':visible'))
                    $videoModal.find('.close').click();
            }

            function uploadCarrierLabelFile () {
                var $carrierLabelImage = $(vm.shipping.imageFile.selector);
                var imageFile = $carrierLabelImage.prop('files')[0];
                if (imageFile == undefined) {
                    $carrierLabelImage.click();
                    return;
                }
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.readAsDataURL(imageFile);
                reader.onload = function () {
                    var dataURL = this.result;
                    getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                        console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                    });

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Upload';
                    vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    vm.load();
                    $carrierLabelImage.val(null);
                }
            }

            function captureImage () {
                // vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector
                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                var track = cameraStream.srcObject.getVideoTracks()[0];
                var imageCapture = new ImageCapture(track);

                imageCapture.grabFrame().then(function(imageBitmap) {
                    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

                    // Set canvas dimensions to match the imageBitmap
                    canvas.width = imageBitmap.width;
                    canvas.height = imageBitmap.height;

                    // Draw the imageBitmap onto the canvas
                    ctx.drawImage(imageBitmap, 0, 0);

                    // Get the image data as a Base64 data URL
                    // You can specify format and quality (e.g., 'image/jpeg', 0.8)
                    const base64DataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png', 1.0);
                    // var newTab = window.open('about:blank','image from canvas');
                    // newTab.document.write("<img src='" + base64DataUrl + "' alt='from canvas'/>");

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                    vm.labelImage = base64DataUrl.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    // vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();
                    vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.stop();
                    vm.load();
                })


                // imageCapture.takePhoto().then(function(blob) {
                //     var reader = new FileReader();
                //     reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
                //     reader.onloadend = function () {
                //         var dataURL = reader.result;
                //         getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                //             console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                //         });

                //         vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                //         vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                //         vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();

                //         vm.load();
                //     }
                // })
            }

            function getMegapixelsFromFileReader(fileData) {
                return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                    var img = new Image();
                    img.src = fileData;
                    img.onload = function () {
                        var width = this.naturalWidth;
                        var height = this.naturalHeight;
                        console.log(`Image dimensions: ${width}x${height}`);
                        var megapixels = (width * height) / 1000000;
                        resolve(megapixels);
                    }
                })
            }

            function videoStreamStop(isCanceled) {
                vm.labelImage = isCanceled ? null : vm.labelImage;

                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                if (cameraStream.srcObject) {
                    var tracks = cameraStream.srcObject.getTracks();
                    tracks.forEach(track => track.stop()); // Stop each track in the stream
                    cameraStream.srcObject = null;
                }
            }


            function videoStreamStart () {
                if (navigator.mediaDevices && navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia) {
                    // Request access to the video stream
                    var constraints = {
                        audio: false,
                        video: {
                            zoom: true,
                            facingMode: 'environment',
                            // aspectRatio: { ideal: 9/16 }
                        }
                    };
                    //HD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 1920 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1080 };

                    //QHD
                    constraints.video.width = { ideal: 2560 };
                    constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1440 };

                    //4K UHD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 3840 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 2160 }

                    navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia(constraints).then(function(stream) {
                        // Assign the stream to the video element's source object
                        var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                        cameraStream.srcObject = stream;

                        var [track] = stream.getVideoTracks();
                        var capabilities = track.getCapabilities();

                        vm.videoModal.zoom ??= {
                            min: capabilities.zoom.min,
                            max: capabilities.zoom.max,
                            current: track.getSettings().zoom
                        }
                        var zoomLevel = localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel') ?? getZoomLevel(track.getSettings().zoom);

                        track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                        vm.videoModal.track = track;
                        // if (capabilities.zoom) {
                        //     track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: capabilities.zoom.max }] });
                        // }
                    }).catch(function(error) {
                        console.error("Error accessing the camera: ", error);
                    });
                } else {
                    // Fallback for older browsers
                    console.error("Your browser does not support the getUserMedia API.");
                }

                function getZoomLevel(currentZoom) {
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', currentZoom);
                    return currentZoom;
                }
            }

            function zoomOut() {
                // localStorage.setItem("settings", JSON.stringify(userSettings));
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel > vm.videoModal.zoom.min) {
                    zoomLevel -= 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

            function zoomIn() {
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel < vm.videoModal.zoom.max) {
                    zoomLevel += 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

            function loadShip(shipmentRequest) {
                debugger;
                vm.load();
                if (vm.shipping.customer.autoShip) {
                    vm.intervalId = setInterval(function(shipmentRequest) {
                        console.log(shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment)
                        if (shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment) {
                            clearInterval(vm.intervalId);
                            // if(!(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage ?? '').includes('Invalid Service Option'))
                                vm.ship();
                        }
                    }, 20, shipmentRequest)
                }
            }
        }

// history() // returns undefined
function history() {
            vm.history = {
                searchButton: 'button:contains("Search")',
                reportSelector: '#reports'
            };

            $(document).on('click', vm.history.searchButton, selectReportChange);
            $(document).on('change', vm.history.reportSelector, selectReportChange);

            activate();

            function activate() {
                if (vm.profile.Name != vm.thinClient.adminProfileName) {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = true;

                    let reports = [ 'Default', 'Detailed Report', 'Void Report', 'Summary Report' ];
                    vm.reports = vm.reports.filter(function(report) {
                        report.TemplateHtml = report.TemplateHtml.replace(/<span.*glyphicon-search.*<\/span>/g, '');
                        return reports.includes(report.Name);
                    });
                }
            }

            function selectReportChange(event) {
                if (vm.report?.Name == 'Summary Report') {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = true;
                    vm.history.carrierAcceptTableContainer = {
                        'height': $('.panel-body').height() + 'px',
                        'overflow-y': 'auto'
                    };

                    let payload = {
                        Action: 'summaryReport',
                        Data: {
                            startDate: vm.dtstart.toLocaleDateString('en-CA'),
                            endDate: vm.dtend.toLocaleDateString('en-CA'),
                            sites: getSites()
                        }
                    };
                    let data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                    thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                        debugger;
                        vm.history.carrierAcceptReport = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));
                        vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                    });
                } else {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = false;
                }

                function getSites() {
                    let sites = vm.UserInformation.SiteId ? vm.sites.filter(function(site) { return site.Id == vm.UserInformation.SiteId;}) : vm.sites;
                    return sites.map(function(site) { return { name: site.Name }; });
                }
            }
        }

// thinClientApiRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns undefined
function thinClientApiRequest(method, data, isAsync) {
    $.getJSON('config.json', function (config) {
        let shipExecServiceUrl = config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        let authorizationToken = shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http')
            ? { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token }
            : '';
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken });
    });
}

		}
		
		return userEmail;
	}

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {   
        debugger;
        var usCountry = "UNITED_STATES";
        var usAcronym = "US";
        var PackageRequests=shipmentRequest.Packages;
        
        $(PackageRequests).each(function (x, item)
          {
              var value = item.DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount;
              var tN = item.AesTransactionNumber;
              if (value >= 2500 && tN ===null)
              {
                    alert("Please check with clarios-na-trade@clarios.com if EEI filing is needed");
              }             
             item.Description=$('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val();
            
          });
          
          // For International Destination Rule Applies to all use cases and all carriers
          if ((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usCountry) && (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usAcronym))
                {
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "Y";
                }
                else
                {
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "N";
                }
             
    }

// function CloseAllShippers() // returns undefined
function CloseAllShippers() {
        debugger;
        
        var getManifestItemsList,getManifestItemsemethod,methodParams,authorizationToken;
        var allOrdersSelectedCarrier = [];
        var allShipperSelectedCarrier,getShipperCarriersmethod,getShipperCarriersmethodParams,CloseAllShippersResponse,CloseAllShippersResults
        
            getShipperCarriersmethod='api/ShippingService/GetShipperCarriers';
            getManifestItemsemethod='api/ShippingService/GetManifestItems';
            authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
            
        
            let selectedValCarrier = AllCarriersList.find(Carriers => Carriers.Id == $("#CarriersList option:selected").val()).Symbol;
           
            $.each(Array(AllShipperList.length), function(i)
            {
                
                 getShipperCarriersmethodParams = {"ShipperId":AllShipperList[i].Id,"CompanyId":userContextDetails.CompanyId};
                 allShipperSelectedCarrier =  $.post({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getShipperCarriersmethod, data: getShipperCarriersmethodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
    
               if(allShipperSelectedCarrier.Carriers && allShipperSelectedCarrier.Carriers.length !=0){ 
               
                    methodParams = {"Carrier":selectedValCarrier,"Shipper":AllShipperList[i].Symbol,"SearchCriteria":{"OrderByClauses":[{"FieldName":"ShipDate","Direction":"DESC"}]},"IncludeImported":false,"CompanyId":userContextDetails.CompanyId};
                    getManifestItemsList =  $.post({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getManifestItemsemethod, data: methodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
                    
                   
                    if(getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems && getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length !=0)
                    {
                        debugger;
                      var CloseManifestmethod,methodParams,CloseAllShippersResults
                        CloseManifestmethod='api/ShippingService/CloseManifest';
                         $.each(Array(getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length), function(j)
                          {
                                  
                                  
                                   allOrdersSelectedCarrier.push({"Attributes":getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Attributes,"ShipDate":getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].ShipDate,"Symbol":getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Symbol,"Name":getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Name});
                              });
                              methodParams ={"Carrier":selectedValCarrier,"ManifestItems":allOrdersSelectedCarrier,"Shipper":AllShipperList[i].Symbol,"Print":true,"UserParams":{},"CompanyId":userContextDetails.CompanyId};
                              CloseAllShippersResponse =  $.post({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + CloseManifestmethod, data: methodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
                              allOrdersSelectedCarrier = [];
                    }
               }
               
          
            });
            
            if(CloseAllShippersResponse != undefined)
            {
                    if(CloseAllShippersResponse.ErrorCode==-1){
                            
                             $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').show();
                             $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                             $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                             $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                                 
                             ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');
                            
                        }else
                        {
                                CloseAllShippersResults = CloseAllShippersResponse.CloseManifestResults[0].ErrorCode;
                                if(CloseAllShippersResults!=0){
                                    
                                      $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').hide();
                                      $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').show();
                                      $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                                      $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                                      
                                      ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');
                                     
                                }else if(CloseAllShippersResults==0){
                                    
                                     $('#divsuccessfulAllShippers').show();
                                     $('#divsuccessfulAllShippersAndAllCarriers').hide();
                                     
                                      ShowAlert('successfulModalCloseShippers');
                                     
                                }
                        }
           }else
           {
                             $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').show();
                             $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                             $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                             $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                                 
                             ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers'); 
                            
           }
                         
       $('#loaderspinnerImg').hide();
       
        
    }

// Source: Clarios (CLRS)_Clarios_Rule_Paperless_2440.cs
// function CloseAllShippers() // returns undefined
    function CloseAllShippers() {
        debugger;

        var getManifestItemsList, getManifestItemsemethod, methodParams, authorizationToken;
        var allOrdersSelectedCarrier = [];
        var allShipperSelectedCarrier, getShipperCarriersmethod, getShipperCarriersmethodParams, CloseAllShippersResponse, CloseAllShippersResults

        getShipperCarriersmethod = 'api/ShippingService/GetShipperCarriers';
        getManifestItemsemethod = 'api/ShippingService/GetManifestItems';
        authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();


        let selectedValCarrier = AllCarriersList.find(Carriers => Carriers.Id == $("#CarriersList option:selected").val()).Symbol;

        $.each(Array(AllShipperList.length), function (i) {

            getShipperCarriersmethodParams = { "ShipperId": AllShipperList[i].Id, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
            allShipperSelectedCarrier = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getShipperCarriersmethod, data: getShipperCarriersmethodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;

            if (allShipperSelectedCarrier.Carriers && allShipperSelectedCarrier.Carriers.length != 0) {

                methodParams = { "Carrier": selectedValCarrier, "Shipper": AllShipperList[i].Symbol, "SearchCriteria": { "OrderByClauses": [{ "FieldName": "ShipDate", "Direction": "DESC" }] }, "IncludeImported": false, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
                getManifestItemsList = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getManifestItemsemethod, data: methodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;


                if (getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems && getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length != 0) {
                    debugger;
                    var CloseManifestmethod, methodParams, CloseAllShippersResults
                    CloseManifestmethod = 'api/ShippingService/CloseManifest';
                    $.each(Array(getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length), function (j) {


                        allOrdersSelectedCarrier.push({ "Attributes": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Attributes, "ShipDate": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].ShipDate, "Symbol": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Symbol, "Name": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Name });
                    });
                    methodParams = { "Carrier": selectedValCarrier, "ManifestItems": allOrdersSelectedCarrier, "Shipper": AllShipperList[i].Symbol, "Print": true, "UserParams": {}, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
                    CloseAllShippersResponse = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + CloseManifestmethod, data: methodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
                    allOrdersSelectedCarrier = [];
                }
            }


        });

        if (CloseAllShippersResponse != undefined) {
            if (CloseAllShippersResponse.ErrorCode == -1) {

                $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').show();
                $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();

                ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');

            } else {
                CloseAllShippersResults = CloseAllShippersResponse.CloseManifestResults[0].ErrorCode;
                if (CloseAllShippersResults != 0) {

                    $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').hide();
                    $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').show();
                    $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                    $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();

                    ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');

                } else if (CloseAllShippersResults == 0) {

                    $('#divsuccessfulAllShippers').show();
                    $('#divsuccessfulAllShippersAndAllCarriers').hide();

                    ShowAlert('successfulModalCloseShippers');

                }
            }
        } else {
            $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').show();
            $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
            $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
            $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();

            ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');

        }

        $('#loaderspinnerImg').hide();


    }

        closeallgetManifestItemsemethod = 'api/ShippingService/GetManifestItems';

        var allOrdersSelectedCarrierfromallclose = [];
        debugger;

        $.each(Array(AllCarriersList.length), function (k) {
            $.each(Array(AllShipperList.length), function (i) {
                var getShipperCarriersmethodParameters = { "ShipperId": AllShipperList[i].Id, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
                authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
                var allShipperallCarrierSelectedCarrier = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getallShipperallCarriersmethod, data: getShipperCarriersmethodParameters, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;

                if (allShipperallCarrierSelectedCarrier.Carriers && allShipperallCarrierSelectedCarrier.Carriers.length != 0) {

                    var closeallmethodParams = { "Carrier": AllCarriersList[k].Symbol, "Shipper": AllShipperList[i].Symbol, "SearchCriteria": { "OrderByClauses": [{ "FieldName": "ShipDate", "Direction": "DESC" }] }, "IncludeImported": false, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
                    var getManifestItemsList = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + closeallgetManifestItemsemethod, data: closeallmethodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;

                    if (getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems && getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length != 0) {
                        var CloseManifestmethod, methodParams, authorizationToken, CloseAllShippersResults
                        authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();

                        $.each(Array(getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length), function (j) {

                            allOrdersSelectedCarrierfromallclose.push({ "Attributes": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Attributes, "ShipDate": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].ShipDate, "Symbol": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Symbol, "Name": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Name });
                        });

                        CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResponse = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + CloseAllShippersAllCarriermethod, data: closeallmethodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
                        allOrdersSelectedCarrierfromallclose = [];
                    }
                }
            });
        });

        if (CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResponse != undefined) {
            if (CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResponse.ErrorCode == -1) {

                $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').show();
                $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();

                ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');
            } else {
                CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResults = CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResponse.CloseManifestResults[0].ErrorCode;
                if (CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResults != 0) {

                    $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').hide();
                    $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                    $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                    $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').show();

                    ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');
                } else if (CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResults == 0) {

                    $('#divsuccessfulAllShippers').hide();
                    $('#divsuccessfulAllShippersAndAllCarriers').show();

                    ShowAlert('successfulModalCloseShippers');
                }
            }
        } else {

            $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').hide();
            $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
            $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').show();
            $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();

            ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');
        }
        $('#loaderspinnerImg').hide();


    }

this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
      var DIUnit = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight.Units;
      var DIWt = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight.Amount;
      var DINote = "Incorrect shipping of Dry Ice can result in fines upward of $75,000 for each violation as well as cancellation of shipping privileges for all of Conagra Brands. Please contact DL-SmallParcelDeliveryService@conagra.com with questions or for specific instructions and restrictions";
   //   alert(DIUnit);
   //   alert(DIWt);
   //   alert(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight));
  for (var index = 0; index < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; ++index) {  
    switch(shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Units) {
      case "LB":
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 5.5) {
            alert(DINote);
            throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
          
        }
      break;
      case "KG":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 2.49476) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      case "G":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 2494.76) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      case "OZ":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 88) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      default:

    }}

    };

            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = null;
        }

    }

// PullCustomData(consignee, field) // returns the matching custom data value or undefined
        function PullCustomData(consignee, field){
            //alert(JSON.stringify(consignee));
            
            for(var item in consignee){
                if(consignee[item].Key==field)return consignee[item].Value;
            }
        }

// Source: Epiq Bankruptcy Services (EPIQ)_Epiq CBR with UserContext Fix 2.0_1805.cs
// GetRequestHeaders() // returns an object containing HTTP authorization headers
    GetRequestHeaders()
    {
      //get the bearer token from local storage
      let _authToken = null;
      let _token = window.localStorage.getItem('TCToken') || null;
      if (_token) { _authToken = $.parseJSON(_token).access_token; }

      return { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + _authToken };
    }

// Source: Epiq Bankruptcy Services (EPIQ)_Epiq CBR with UserContext Fix_1792.cs
// async Start(callback) // returns undefined
    async Start(callback)
    {
      debugger;
      let that = this;
      if (this.UserInformation)
      {
        let u = {};
        u.CompanyId = this.UserInformation.CompanyId || null;
        u.UserId = this.UserInformation.UserId || null;
        u.SiteId = this.UserInformation.SitdId || null;
        this.UserContext = u;
      }

      //use localStorage for UserMethodUrl and UserContextUrl
      if (window.localStorage.getItem('cbrValues'))
      {
        let cbr = $.parseJSON(window.localStorage.getItem('cbrValues'));
        this.UserContextUrl = decodeURIComponent(cbr.UserContextUrl) || null;
        this.UserMethodUrl = decodeURIComponent(cbr.UserMethodUrl) || null;
      }

      //check for the two items that we need.  if they exist, no need to go further.
      if (this.UserContext && this.UserContext.CompanyId && this.UserMethodUrl)
      {
        if ($.isFunction(callback)) callback(true);
      }

      //nothing found in localStorage, add stuff.
      that.GetJsonConfig().then(function(data)
      {
        let _rootUrl = new URL(data.ShipExecServiceUrl).origin;

        that.UserContextUrl = _rootUrl + '/api/usercontext/GET';
        that.UserMethodUrl = _rootUrl + '/api/ShippingService/UserMethod';

        //write the values to local storage
        let cbr = {};
        cbr.UserContextUrl = encodeURIComponent(that.UserContextUrl);
        cbr.UserMethodUrl = encodeURIComponent(that.UserMethodUrl);
        window.localStorage.setItem('cbrValues', JSON.stringify(cbr));

        //this is actually a set/get for the class var
        that.GetUserContext().then(function() { if ($.isFunction(callback)) callback(true); });
      });
    }

// Source: F Schumacher (FSCHUMAC)_Product Area (8942X4) CBR with PV_1816.cs
// GetCallingFunctionName() // returns the calling function name string or an empty string
  function GetCallingFunctionName ()
  {
    try
    {
      throw new Error();
    }
    catch (e)
    {
      try
      {
        return e.stack.split('at ')[3].split(' ')[0] + '()';
      }
      catch (e)
      {
        return '';
      }
    }
  }

// CheckForMatchingConsignee(CustomerOrderObject) // returns boolean
      CheckForMatchingConsignee: function(CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');
          var a = {
            conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5).toUpperCase()
          };

          var hdr = CustomerOrderObject.Header;
          console.log(hdr);
          var b = {
            conCompany: hdr.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conAddress1: hdr.CONSIGNEE_ADDRESS_LINE_1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: hdr.CONSIGNEE_CITY.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: hdr.CONSIGNEE_STATEPROVINCE.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: hdr.CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE.trim().substring(0, 5).toUpperCase()
          };

          /* Remove all the spaces in the strings so we get a good comparison, not one that's thrown off by an extra space. */
          let aa = JSON.stringify(a).replaceAll(' ', '');
          let bb = JSON.stringify(b).replaceAll(' ', '');

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          if (aa != bb)
          {
            console.log(`CheckForMatchingConsignee(), Message: Could not add order ${CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber} (${CustomerOrderObject.orderId}). Primary order data to follow.`);
            console.log('Primary order: ', a);
            console.log('Secondary order: ', b);
          }

          return aa == bb;
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          console.log(error.message);
        }
      }

// Source: F Schumacher (FSCHUMAC)_Samples Area (7F4175) PROD CBR_2449.cs
// SetServerDebugMode(writeToServer) // returns undefined
      SetServerDebugMode: function (writeToServer)
      {
        console.log('Logging to server: ' + writeToServer);
        serverLogging = writeToServer;
      },

// GetServerDebugMode() // returns the current server debug mode flag
      GetServerDebugMode: function ()
      {
        return serverLogging;
      },

// Log(LogObject) // returns undefined
      Log: function (LogObject)
      {
        try
        {
          /*
          Usage:
            Errors:
              try {
                ...
              } catch (error) {
                Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Error: error });
                OR
                Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Error: { name: 'Error name', message: 'Error message' } });
                OR 
                Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Error: { name: 'Error name', message: 'Error message' }, Data: 'Simple or complex data object.' });
              }

            Info (default, no 'Type' needed):
              Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Message: 'Test of server info logging', Data: 'Simple or complex data object.' });

            All others:
              Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Type: 'Trace', Message: 'Test of server info logging with a complex data object.', Data: SessionData.GetCurrentUserContext() });
              Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Type: 'Fatal', Message: 'Test of server info logging with a simple data string.', Data: 'Simple data string literal.' });
              Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Type: 'Debug', Message: 'Test of server debug logging with no data object.' });
          */

          /* If the LogObject has an 'error' object, set the LogLevel here.  This makes the LogLevel variable optional for errors. */
          if (LogObject.Error)
          {
            LogObject.LogLevel = LogLevel.Error;

            /* Can't pass the error container to the server without preparing it inside a new object first. */
            var e = {};
            e.name = LogObject.Error.name;
            e.message = LogObject.Error.message;
            LogObject.Error = e;
          }
          else if (!LogObject.LogLevel)
          {
            /* If the LogObject does NOT have an 'error' object AND there is no LogLevel set, use .Info.  This makes the LogLevel variable optional for info logging. */
            LogObject.LogLevel = LogLevel.Info;
          }

          /* All logging will go to the console, output here. */
          switch (LogObject.LogLevel)
          {
            case LogLevel.Error:

              console.error('Exception encountered in', LogObject.Source);
              console.error(LogObject.Error.name);
              console.error(LogObject.Error.message);

              /* Use .trace if needed but within the Angular sandbox the .trace object can be huge and convoluted. */
              /* Be careful if passing .trace data on to the server as it will contain various data types and directives. */
              //console.error(LogObject.Error.trace);

              /* Don't use console.error for the data object, it causes readability issues. */
              if (LogObject.Data) { console.log(LogObject.Data); }
              break;

            /* Using the same nomenclature used by SBR logging. */
            case LogLevel.Info:
            case LogLevel.Debug:
            case LogLevel.Trace:
            case LogLevel.Fatal:
            default:

              console.log('Output from', LogObject.Source);
              console.log(LogObject.Message);
              if (LogObject.Data) { console.log(LogObject.Data); }
              break;
          }

          if (Tools.GetServerDebugMode() == true)
          {
            var dataObject = {
              ServerMethod: 'AddClientEntry',
              MessageObject: LogObject
            };

            var ajaxObject = {
              UserContext: Tools.GetCurrentUserContext(),
              Data: JSON.stringify(dataObject)
            };

            /* async doesn't necessarily need to be set to false here but I think it helps with data collisions and getting the error messages to appear in chronological order on the server. */
            var ajaxRequest = $.ajax({
              url: 'api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
              method: 'POST',
              contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
              dataType: 'json',
              data: ajaxObject,
              async: true
            });

            ajaxRequest.done(function (json)
            {
              /* There is no return for this call, if the POST does come back with data, it's a server message/error like 'UserContext cannot be null' or more likely '{"Data":"","ErrorCode":0}' */
              //console.log(JSON.parse(json.Data));
            });

            ajaxRequest.fail(function (jqXHR, textStatus)
            {
              console.log('Unable to log message to server.');
              console.log(jqXHR);
              console.log(textStatus);
            });

            ajaxRequest.always(function (jqXHR, textStatus, jqXHRError) 
            {

            });
          }

          /* Need to hide the loader outside the decision trees. */
          Tools.HideLoader();

        }
        catch (error)
        {
          console.log(error.message);
        }
      }

// Source: FalconNDX (FNDX)_Falcon_CBR_1794.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) { 
        debugger;
        
        //Days List
        const days = ["Sunday","Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday"];
         
        // Current Date
        var dt = new Date();  
       //dt.setDate(dt.getDate()  +1);
        //alert(dt);
        
        //Finding Last Date of the Month
        var lastDate=new Date(dt.getFullYear(),dt.getMonth()+1 ,0);
        var onlyDate_lastDate= lastDate.getDate();
       
        
          
        //Months List  
        var month= dt.getMonth()+1;
        var nextmonth =dt.getMonth()+1;  //Get the current month
        
        
        //Year
        var currentYear = dt.getFullYear();
  
        
        
                
        var nextdate=dt.getDate()+1;    
        var newdate=dt.getDate()+2;
        
        
        
        /* Comparing current date(saturday/sunday) with lastdate of the month
        1. Current date and last date is saturday 
        2. Next to Current date and last date is saturday */
        
        /* Scenarios
        1. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Sunday 
            Next to current date should match with last date.
        2. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Sunday
            Current date should match with last date.
        3. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Saturday
        4. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Saturday
        
        
        
        */
        
       if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=2;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
       
     
      else if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
              
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
        else if(nextdate == onlyDate_lastDate )  
       {
            
             if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
             
           
       }
       
     //Saturday to Monday 
       var monthIndex = nextmonth;
                if(monthIndex<10)
                monthIndex=('0'+monthIndex);
                
       var mondateIndex=newdate;
                if(mondateIndex<10)
                mondateIndex=('0'+mondateIndex);
                
       var lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
        
     if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
        {
            lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
            $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
        }
         
         
      
      //Sunday to Monday   
         var sundateIndex=dt.getDate();
       
         if(dt.getDate()==onlyDate_lastDate)
            {
              
                 sundateIndex=newdate;   
                   
            }
            else
            {
               
                sundateIndex=dt.getDate()+1;
            }

        
          if(sundateIndex<10)
            sundateIndex=('0'+sundateIndex);
                     
           if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
            {
                 lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+sundateIndex);
                 $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
            }
           
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        vm = this.vm;
        console.log(vm);
        GetUserContext();
        if(location === '/shipping'){
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $terms = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms"]');
                var loaded = $terms.length;
                if (loaded) {
                    //removeDropDown();
                    
                    $('body').delegate('#AddMultiplePackages', 'click', function () {
                        AddMultiplePackagesModel();
                    });
                    
                     $('body').delegate('#MultiCloseModal', 'click', function () {
                        MultiCloseModal();
                    });
                    
                    $('body').delegate('#AddMultiPackagesReal', 'click', function () {
                        AddMultiPackagesReal();
                    });
                    
                    clearInterval(interval);
                }
            }, 50);
            
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        debugger;
        vm = this.vm;
        vm.xReceiverAccountsIsHidden = true;
        vm.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddressCodesIsHidden = true;


        vm.xReceiverAccounts = getReceiverAccounts();
        if (pageLoaded) {
            vm.xThirdPartyCode = tpbTransportationChargesAddressBookEntries;
        }
        var originCustomData = GetCustomData(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
        //if (typeof shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress !== "undefined") shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Code = "";
    };

// TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddressChange() // returns undefined
    this.TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddressChange = function () {
        debugger;
        this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
        this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = this.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress;
        this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress = this.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress;
    }

            // Domestic Tab

            var tpbSelectedIndex = 0;

            // International Tab

                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').show();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Who pays Duties and Taxes")').hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Who pays Duties and Taxes")').hide();

            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress1"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'change', function () {
                $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] button[title="Search Addresses"]').click();
            });

            var startTime = new Date();
            var pageLoaded = setInterval(function () {
                if ((new Date().getTime() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000 >= 2) {
                    clearInterval(pageLoaded);
                    //    console.log('clearinterval');
                } else {
                    var tpbFound = false;
                    var consigneeFound = false;
                    var $thirdPartyBillingAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"]');

                    var tpbSearchAddress = $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]');
                    var $consignee = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                    var consineeSearchAddress = $consignee.find('[title="Search Addresses"]');
                    if ($thirdPartyBillingAddress.length && tpbSearchAddress.length) {
                        tpbFound = true;
                    }

                    if ($consignee.length && consineeSearchAddress.length) {
                        consigneeFound = true;
                    }
                    var loaded = tpbFound && consigneeFound;


                    // console.log(`is consignee loaded: ${loaded}`)

                    if (loaded) {
                        if ($thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').length > 0) {
                            startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Validate Address"]').hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.IsUpdateAddressBookEntry"]').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();

                            $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();

                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Validate Address"]').hide();

                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.IsUpdateAddressBookEntry"]').hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();

                            $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();

                        }
                    }
                }
            }, 125);
        }
    };

// getAddressBookEntries(addressBookName, context) // returns array or undefined
    function getAddressBookEntries(addressBookName, context) {
        var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Name", FieldValue: addressBookName, Operator: 0 }] };
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
        debugger;
        //var response = ajaxPost('GetAddressBooks', data);
        var response = thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_Shared', data, false);
        debugger;
        if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
            var addressBookEntry = { Code: 'Error: AddressBook "' + addressBookName + '" Not Found' };
            return [addressBookEntry];
        } else {
            var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;

            searchCriteria = { OrderByClauses: [{ FieldName: "Code", Direction: "asc", FieldType: 3 }] };
            data = { AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
            //response = ajaxPost('GetAddressBookEntries', data);
            response = thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false);
            debugger;
            if (response.TotalRecords > 0) {
                return response.AddressBookEntries;
            }
        }
    }

// ajaxPost(url, payLoad) // returns results
    function ajaxPost(url, payLoad) {
        var results;
        debugger;
        $.ajax({
            type: 'POST',
            url: `api/ShippingService/${url}`,
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'json',
            //data: Object.assign({ UserContext: userContext }, payLoad),
            data: Object.assign({ CompanyId: userContext.CompanyId, UserId: userContext.UserId }, payLoad),
            success: function (response) {
                results = response;
            },
            error: function (error) {
                results = error.responseText;
            }
        });
        return results;
    }

// checkAndSetShipDateTest(viewModel) // returns undefined
function checkAndSetShipDateTest(viewModel)
		{
			debugger;
			var hardCutoffTime = 16;
			var currentDateTime = new Date();
			var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();
			
			if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
				var finalDate = addDays(2);
				console.log("New date" + finalDate);
				var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
				var day = finalDate.getDate();
				var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
				console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
				//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
				var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
				viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
				shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
			}
			
			if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
				if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
					var finalDate = addDays(3);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
				else{
					var finalDate = addDays(1);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
			}
			
		}

                        $("#dateDiv").show();
                    }
                };
            }
        });
        
    };

// GetShipToAddressCustomData() // returns custom data from the first address book entry
        this.GetShipToAddressCustomData = function(){
        //debugger;
        var payloadShipToAddress = {
            "Skip": 0,
            "Take": 10,
            "WhereClauses": [{
                "FieldName": "Id",
                "FieldValue": consigneeId,
                "Operator": 0
            }]
        };
        
        var data = {
            CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
            addressBookIds: addrsBookId,
            SearchCriteria: payloadShipToAddress
        };
        //console.log(data);
      
        ShipToAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', data, false).responseJSON;
    
        console.log(ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[0].CustomData);
        
        return ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[0].CustomData;
                
    };

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
        debugger;
        const st_company = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company.toUpperCase();
        addrsBookId = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.AddressBookId;

            if(mi_flag !== "MI_TPB"){
               throw new Error("Please contact GAP ShipExec Admin for Mail Innovation Authorization [Ship-Exec-stores-dg@gap.com].");
            }
            else
            {
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = {
                    Company : "UPS Mail Innovations",
                    Contact : "Shipping",
                    Address1 : "13050 Marlay Ave",

                    City : "Fontana",

                    PostalCode : "92337",
                    Country : "US",

                };

        }

        if (pooler)
        {
            if (document.getElementById("pooler").checked)
            {

                {
                    p.MiscReference4 = vm.profile.Shippers[0].Email.replace("@", "").replace(" ", "").replace(".pool", "").replace(".POOL", "").toUpperCase();
                }

        }

        var misc3reference = "200.30.6035.5102.90059";
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = "";
            //Address 1
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "1112 Turkey Mountain Rd.")
            {
                console.log('found 1/4 address');
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
            }
             //Address 2
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "102R Demi Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
              //Address 3
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "17511 S. Susana Rd.")
            {

            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;

        }
        console.log('PRESHIP');
        console.log(shipmentRequest);

    };

// Source: GAP (GAP)_Rule with Mail Innov. Billing_1888.cs
// selectCanadaForAllCountrySelects() // returns void
function selectCanadaForAllCountrySelects() {
        // Check if the flag is already true, which means we no longer need to change the selects
        if(canadaSelected || !isSelectedValueInShippersArray()) {
          return; // Exit the function if Canada has been selected in all dropdowns or if the site is not from Canada
        }
        
        // Get all select elements with the name 'Country'
        var selects = document.querySelectorAll('select[name="Country"]');
        var allSelected = true; // To keep track if all selects have been set to Canada
      
        // Iterate through the NodeList
        selects.forEach(function(select) {
          // Only set the value to 'string:CA' if it's not already set
          if (select.value !== 'string:CA') {
            select.value = 'string:CA';
            allSelected = false; // Not all selects have been set to Canada
      
            // Trigger change event for AngularJS
            if ('createEvent' in document) {
              var evt = document.createEvent('HTMLEvents');
              evt.initEvent('change', false, true);
              select.dispatchEvent(evt);
            } else {
              select.fireEvent('onchange');
            }
          }
        });
      
        // If all selects have been set to Canada, set the flag to true
        if (allSelected) {
          canadaSelected = true;
        }
      }

// isSelectedValueInShippersArray() // returns boolean
function isSelectedValueInShippersArray() {
        // Use a more specific selector that targets the ng-model
        var selectElement = document.querySelector('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]');
        
        // Ensure the element exists
        if (!selectElement) {
          console.warn('Select element not found');
          return false;
        }
        
        // Get the index of the selected option
        var selectedIndex = selectElement.selectedIndex;
        
        // Ensure an option is selected
        if (selectedIndex < 0) {
          console.warn('No option is selected');
          return false;
        }
        
        // Get the selected option element
        var selectedOption = selectElement.options[selectedIndex];
        
        // Get the value of the selected option (and remove the "string:" prefix if present)
        var selectedValue = selectedOption.value.replace('string:', '');
        
        // Check if the selected value is in the array
        return StoreLocationsCanadaArray.includes(selectedValue);
      }

// GetUserName() // returns regex match array or null
function GetUserName() {
   var helloUser = $('a[title="Manage"]:contains("Hello")').text();
   return helloUser.match(/[a-zA-Z]+[a-zA-Z0-9._]+@[a-zA-Z]+\.[a-zA-Z.]{2,5}/i);
}

// OnCboReturnAddressChange() // returns void
    const OnCboReturnAddressChange = () => 
	{		
		//debugger;
		
		var selectedReturnAddress = $("#cboPredefinedReturnAddress select").val().replace('string:', '');
		
		returnAddressList = GetReturnAddresses();
		
		 if ($.isEmptyObject(returnAddressList) === false)
		 {					
			if (returnAddressList!=undefined)
			{
				var returnAddress = returnAddressList.find(x => x.ReturnLocationDescription === selectedReturnAddress);
				
				if (returnAddress !== undefined)
				{
					//debugger;

					CopyReturnAddressToOriginAddress();
					
				}
			} 
		 }								
	}

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
        vm = this.vm;
		
        ConfigureD2MShipment("this.NewShipment");
		
        this.vm.PredefinedReturnAddress =  GetReturnAddresses();

								var tabIsLoaded = $("#cboPredefinedReturnAddress select");
		
								if (tabIsLoaded)
								{
									clearInterval(returnTabInterval);
									if (IsEventAttached($("#cboPredefinedReturnAddress select"), "change", OnCboReturnAddressChange) === false)
									{			
										debugger;
										$("#cboPredefinedReturnAddress select").on("change", OnCboReturnAddressChange);														
									}									
							}
						},50);				
    }

// IsEventAttached($element, elementEvent, elementEventHandler) // returns boolean
    function IsEventAttached($element, elementEvent, elementEventHandler)
	{			
		debugger;
		
		var result = false;
					
		if (($("#cboPredefinedReturnAddress select").get(0) != undefined) && ($._data($element.get(0), "events") != undefined))
		{
			var elementEvents = $._data($element.get(0), "events");
			elementEventHandler = elementEventHandler.toString();
			result = (elementEvents && elementEvents[elementEvent]?.some(ev => ev.handler.toString() === elementEventHandler))
		}
		
		return result;
	}

// ConfigureD2MShipment(calleeMethod) // returns void
    function ConfigureD2MShipment(calleeMethod){
        
        debugger;
        		
		LogStartMethod("ConfigureD2MShipment()",calleeMethod);
				
		var infoMessage = "D2M shipment ";
		
		if (location.hash === '#!/shipping')		
		{
			if (CurrentShipperIsD2MEnabled() && CurrentUserIsD2MEnabled()) 
			{
				infoMessage += "is ENABLED for current shipper and current user";
				
				var originAddressCompany;
				
				var originAddressLoadedInterval = setInterval(function(){
					originAddressCompany = $('[name="company"]:eq(1)').val();
					if (originAddressCompany!=undefined && originAddressCompany.length)
					{
						EnableReturn();
						clearInterval(originAddressLoadedInterval);	
					}
				},50);
			}
			else
			{
				infoMessage += "is NOT ENABLED for shipper and user";
				var isLoaded;
				var removeD2M = setInterval(function(){
					isLoaded = $('#DirectToMobileShipmentID').is(":checked");
					if (isLoaded!=undefined && (isLoaded === false || isLoaded === false))
					{												
						$('#d2m_checkbox_div_id').remove();						
						DisableReturn();
						clearInterval(removeD2M);	
					}
				},50);
				
				
			}
		}
		else
		{
			infoMessage = "WARNING " + infoMessage + "called outside of shipping action";
		}
		LogMethodInfo(infoMessage);
    }

  this.PageLoaded = function (location)

      });
    }

    {
      console.log(userContext)
      $('body').delegate('#voidBReference', 'click', function ()
      {
        voidBatchJS(this);
      });

      $('body').delegate('#printPSlip', 'change', function ()
      {
        console.log("I have been changed..." + $('#printPSlip').is(":checked"))
      })
    }
    if (location === '/history')
    {
      $('body').delegate('.void-all-btn', 'click', function (e)
      {
        VoidAll(e.currentTarget);
      });

      $('body').delegate('.RePrint-AMP-btn', 'click', function (e)
      {
        RePrintAMP(e.currentTarget);
      });

      // $('body').delegate('#VoidAll', 'click', function ()
      // {
      //   VoidAll(this);
      // });
      $('body').delegate('#CancelCloseModal', 'click', function ()
      {
        CloseModalClose();
      });
      $('body').delegate('#VoidReal', 'click', function ()
      {
        VoidReal();
      });
    }
    if (location === '/shipping')
    {
      var interval = setInterval(function ()
      {
        var $service = $('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]');
        var loaded = $service.length;
        if (loaded)
        {
          $('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').removeClass("service");

          {
            AddMultiplePackagesModel();

          });

          $('body').delegate('#Split', 'click', function ()
          {
            Split();
          });

          $('body').delegate('#AddAll', 'click', function ()
          {
            AddAll();
          });
          clearInterval(interval);
        }
      }, 50);
    }



  }

// voidBatchJS(batch) // returns undefined
  function voidBatchJS(batch)
  {
    // realizar operaciones aquí con el parámetro batch
    console.log("El botón fue presionado para el lote: ", batch.name);
    var usermethodParams = { "Action": "VoidBatch", "BatchReference": batch.name };

    var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
    var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response)
    {
      if (response.ErrorCode != 0)
      {
        client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
      } else
      {
        $("#TrailerSortCode").val(response.Data);
      }
    });
  }
