// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
  this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    try
    {
      //alert = function(){}
      this.vm.getWeight();

    }
    catch (error)
    {
      console.log("Error getting weight")
    }
    if (!shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1)
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Loaded Value " + loadValue + " not found")
    } else
    {
      const Lines = JSON.parse(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1);
      Lines.forEach(line =>
      {
        const fila = document.createElement("tr");
        fila.innerHTML = `
            <td>${line.LineNo}</td>
            <td>${line.ItemNo}</td>
            <td>${line.TotalOrderQuantity}</td>
            <td>${line.SaleUnitOfMeasure}</td>
            <td>${line.SaleUnitPrice}</td>
            <td>${line.ItemDescription}</td>
            <td></td>
            <td>${line.UnitWeight}</td>
            <td></td>
            <td>0</td>
            <td>0</td>
            <td><button class='btn btn-xs btn-success glyphicon glyphicon-plus'></button></td>
            <td hidden>${line.IsKitOrBundle}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.KitDetails ? JSON.stringify(line.KitDetails) : "[]"}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.CountryOfOrigin : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportCurrencyCode : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportTariffCode : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportUnitPrice : ""}</td>
            `;
        if (line.IsKitOrBundle && line.KitDetails == null)
        {
          client.alert.Danger("WARNING: Kit Details are empty when Commodity Set to Kit");
        }
        document.querySelector("#miTabla").appendChild(fila);
      });
      editableTable();

      const buttons = document.querySelectorAll("#miTabla button");
      buttons.forEach(button =>
      {
        button.addEventListener("click", function ()
        {
          const fila = this.parentElement.parentElement;
          AddCommodity(fila, 1, 0);
        });
      });
      const tabla = document.querySelector("#miTabla");
      tabla.classList.remove("hidden");
    }
    console.log(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate)
    var today = new Date();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Day = today.getDate();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Year = today.getFullYear();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Month = today.getMonth() + 1;
    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != 'US')
    {
      for (var ii = 0; ii < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; ii++)
      {
        shipmentRequest.Packages[ii].CommercialInvoiceMethod = 1;
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country == 'GB')
        {
            console.log(shipmentRequest.Packages[ii]);
            shipmentRequest.Packages[ii].AdditionalHardcopyDocumentation = false;
        }
      }
      
    }

  }

// AddCommodity(fila, Type, newPackageIndex) // returns undefined
  function AddCommodity(fila, Type, newPackageIndex)
  {
    console.log("Trying to get package for index: " + newPackageIndex)
    if (fila.cells[2].textContent == "" || fila.cells[2].textContent == 0)
    {
      client.alert.Danger("No Commodity Left");
      return;
    }
    if (fila.cells[10].textContent == "" || Number(fila.cells[10].textContent) <= 0 || isNaN(fila.cells[10].textContent))
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Invalid Amount to Ship: ");
      return;
    }
    console.log("10: " + fila.cells[10].textContent)
    console.log("2: " + fila.cells[2].textContent)
    if (Number(fila.cells[10].textContent) > Number(fila.cells[2].textContent))
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Ship Quantity can't be more that QTY ");
      return;
    }
    var packageIndex = 0;
    if (Type == 1)
    {
      packageIndex = vm.packageIndex;
    } else
    {
      packageIndex = newPackageIndex;
    }
    console.log(fila.cells[12].textContent ? fila.cells[12].textContent : "Not found in cell 12");
    console.log("Getting isBundle: " + fila.cells[12].textContent)
    if (fila.cells[12] && fila.cells[12].textContent == "true")
    {
      console.log("Bundle")
      console.log(fila.cells[13].textContent)
      var kitDetails = JSON.parse(fila.cells[13].textContent)
      if (kitDetails.length < 1)
      {
        client.alert.Danger("WARNING: Kit Details are empty when Commodity Set to Kit");
        fila.cells[10].textContent = 0;
        return;
      } else
      {
        kitDetails.forEach(detail =>
        {
          console.log(detail)
          console.log(detail.KitComponentPartDesc)
          detail.UnitsPerAssembly = detail.UnitsPerAssembly * fila.cells[10].textContent;
          console.log("Adding units: " + detail.UnitsPerAssembly)
          addToCommodityList(detail, packageIndex, true)
        });
      }
    } else
    {
      console.log("Not bundle")
      addToCommodityList(fila.cells, packageIndex, false)
    }

    fila.cells[2].textContent = fila.cells[2].textContent - fila.cells[10].textContent;
    fila.cells[10].textContent = 0;
    console.log(vm.currentShipment.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents);
  }

// addToCommodityList(cells, index, isBundle) // returns undefined
  function addToCommodityList(cells, index, isBundle)
  {
    var OldCommodity = vm.currentShipment.Packages[index].CommodityContents;
    var NewCommodity;
    let min = 5;
    let max = 100;
    let randomNumber = Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min + 1)) + min;
    let anotherRandom = Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 12);
    if (!cells || cells === "")
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Error: Commodity Data unavailable");
      console.log(cells);
      return;
    }
    if (isBundle)
    {
      let price = 0;
      if (cells.InternationalInfo == null || cells.InternationalInfo.ExportUnitPrice == null)
      {
        price = cells.SaleUnitPrice
        console.log('Value price updated to: ' + price)
      } else
      {
        price = cells.InternationalInfo.ExportUnitPrice
        console.log('Value price updated 2: ' + price)
      }
      NewCommodity = [
        {
          "UnitValue": {
            "Currency": cells.InternationalInfo.ExportCurrencyCode,
            "Amount": price
          },
          "UnitWeight": {
            "Units": "LB",
            "Amount": cells.UnitWeight
          },
          "QuantityUnitMeasure": "PC",
          "ExportQuantityUnitMeasure1": "PC",
          "ExportQuantityUnitMeasure2": "PC",
          "LicenseUnitValue": {
            "Currency": "USD"
          },
          "DdtcUnitMeasure": "PC",
          "packageIndex": index,
          "Origin": {
            "AddressBookIdToProcess": null
          },
          "OriginCountry": cells.InternationalInfo.CountryOfOrigin,
          "ProductCode": cells.KitComponentPart,
          "HarmonizedCode": cells.InternationalInfo.ExportTariffCode,
          "Quantity": cells.UnitsPerAssembly,
          "Description": cells.KitComponentPartDesc,
          "LicenseExpirationDate": null,
          "NaftaRvcAvgStartDate": null,
          "nAFTARVCAvgEndDate": null,
          "$$hashKey": "object:" + index + "1" + anotherRandom
        }];
    } else
    {
      let price = 0;
      if (cells[17].textContent == null || cells[17].textContent == "")
      {
        price = cells[4].textContent
        console.log('Value price updated to: ' + price)
      } else
      {
        price = cells[17].textContent
        console.log('Value price updated 2: ' + price)
      }
      NewCommodity = [
        {
          "UnitValue": {
            "Currency": cells[15].textContent,
            "Amount": price
          },
          "UnitWeight": {
            "Units": "LB",
            "Amount": cells[7].textContent
          },
          "QuantityUnitMeasure": "PC",
          "ExportQuantityUnitMeasure1": "PC",
          "ExportQuantityUnitMeasure2": "PC",
          "LicenseUnitValue": {
            "Currency": cells[16].textContent
          },
          "DdtcUnitMeasure": "PC",
          "packageIndex": index,
          "Origin": {
            "AddressBookIdToProcess": null
          },
          "OriginCountry": cells[14].textContent,
          "ProductCode": cells[1].textContent,
          "HarmonizedCode": cells[16].textContent,
          "Quantity": cells[10].textContent,
          "Description": cells[5].textContent,
          "LicenseExpirationDate": null,
          "NaftaRvcAvgStartDate": null,
          "nAFTARVCAvgEndDate": null,
          "$$hashKey": "object:" + index + "1" + randomNumber
        }];
      //This is wrong an not tested
      //if(line.InternationalDetails!=null && line.InternationalDetails.ExportUnitPrice==null)
      //{
      //    "UnitValue": cells[17].SaleUnitPrice;
      //}
      //else if(line.InternationalDetails!=null && line.InternationalDetails.ExportUnitPrice!=null)
      //{
      //   "UnitValue":cells[15].InternationalInfo.ExportUnitPrice ; 
      //}
    }
    if (!OldCommodity || OldCommodity.length === 0)
    {
      vm.currentShipment.Packages[index].CommodityContents = NewCommodity;
    } else
    {
      vm.currentShipment.Packages[index].CommodityContents = OldCommodity.concat(NewCommodity);
    }
  }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
  this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest)
  {

    var tableHeaderRowCount = 1;
    var table = document.getElementById('miTabla');
    console.log("table size: ")
    if (table && table.rows)
    {
      var rowCount = table.rows.length;
    } else
    {
      var rowCount = 0
    }

    for (var i = tableHeaderRowCount; i < rowCount; i++)
    {
      table.deleteRow(tableHeaderRowCount);
    }

  }

// CallUserMethod(GlobalMSN, Machine) // returns undefined
    function CallUserMethod(GlobalMSN, Machine = ""){
        let usermethodParams = { "Action": "RePrintAMP", "GlobalMSN": GlobalMSN };
        let data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
        console.log(data);
        let response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, true, Machine).done(function (response)
        {
            console.log(response);
            const decodedDataString = decodeHtmlEntities(response.Data);
            const dataObject = JSON.parse(decodedDataString);

            console.log(dataObject);
            dataObject.forEach(item => {
              
              if (item.RawData !== undefined && item.RawData.length > 0){
                  printDocuments(item);
              }
                  
              if (item.PdfData !== undefined && item.PdfData.length > 0) {
                  downloadPdf(item);
              }
              
              if (item.ImageData !== undefined && item.ImageData.length > 0) {
                  client.alert.Danger('Image NOT SUPPORTED');
                  /*TODO download image*/
              }
            });
        });
    }

// RePrintAMP(Package) // returns undefined
    function RePrintAMP(Package){
        let GlobalMSN = $(Package).data('custom-attribute1');
        let Carrier = $(Package).data('custom-attribute2');

        if(!Carrier.includes("CONNECTSHIP") && !Carrier.includes("TANDATA_LTL")){
          alert("Funcionality only support CONNECTSHIP carriers");
          return;
        }
        
        let Machine = '';
        fetch('https://localhost:5001/api/SystemInformation/ComputerName',{
            method:'GET',
        }).then(response => response.json())
        .then(data2 => {
            Machine = data2;
            CallUserMethod(GlobalMSN, Machine)
            
        }).catch(error => {
            console.log(error);
            CallUserMethod(GlobalMSN)
        });
    }

// decodeHtmlEntities(text) // returns decoded string
    function decodeHtmlEntities(text) {
        const element = document.createElement('div');
        element.innerHTML = text;
        return element.textContent;
    }

// downloadPdf(pdfDocuments) // returns undefined
    function downloadPdf(pdfDocuments) {      
      let pdfArray = pdfDocuments.PdfData;
      let documentName = pdfDocuments.DocumentName;
      let file = {};
      console.log(pdfArray.length);
      for (let count = 0; count < pdfArray.length; count++) {
            if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE ") > -1 || navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Trident/") > -1) {
              let byteCharacters = atob(pdfArray[count]);
              let byteNumbers = new Array(byteCharacters.length);
                for (let i = 0; i < byteCharacters.length; i++) {
                    byteNumbers[i] = byteCharacters.charCodeAt(i);
                }
                let byteArray = new Uint8Array(byteNumbers);
                file = new Blob([byteArray], { type: 'application/pdf' });
                window.navigator.msSaveOrOpenBlob(file, documentName + ".pdf");
            } else {
                let documentAfterConversion = base64ToArrayBuffer(pdfArray[count]);
                let a = window.document.createElement("a");
                file = new Blob([documentAfterConversion], { type: 'application/pdf' });
                let fileUrl = URL.createObjectURL(file);
                a.href = fileUrl;
                a.download = documentName + ".pdf";
                document.body.appendChild(a);
                a.click();
                document.body.removeChild(a);
            }          
      }
  }

// base64ToArrayBuffer(base64) // returns ArrayBuffer
  function base64ToArrayBuffer(base64) {
      let binaryString = window.atob(base64);
      let len = binaryString.length;
      let bytes = new Uint8Array(len);
      for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) {
          bytes[i] = binaryString.charCodeAt(i);
      }
      return bytes.buffer;
  }

                        var waitForTable = setInterval(function () {
                            /* The spanTotalBatchItems element text defaults to a value of 0, need to wait until it changes before we continue. */
                            if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) {
                                var currentDate = new Date();
                                var totalBatchItems = parseInt($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text());

                                /* Once this condition is met, we can remove the rows we don't want. */
                                if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) {
                                    clearInterval(waitForTable);
                                    //console.log('table rows condition met.');
                                    /* Loop the table rows. */
                                    $('#tableBatchDetails tr:gt(0)').each(function (x, y) {
                                        var tdDate = new Date($(this).find('td:eq(1)').text());
                                        if (tdDate < currentDate) {
                                            $(this).remove();
                                        }
                                    }).promise().done(function (e) {
                                        $('#tableBatchDetails').show();
                                        var i = $('#tableBatchDetails tr').length;
                                        $('#spanTotalBatchItems').text(i);
                                    });
                                } //end if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) 

                            } //end if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) 

                        }, 250);
                    });

                    /* Event handler for the 'View Labels' button. */
                    $('body').delegate('#buttonViewCheckedLabels', 'click', function (e) {
                        //prevent the subsequent listeners from firing
                        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                        // console.log("Click");
                        ViewCheckedLabels();
                        //   $('#tableBatchDetails').find('input[type=checkbox]:checked').each(function () 
                        //   { 
                        //     ViewCheckedLabels();
                        //   });
                    }); //end button delegate

                    /* Trigger the click of the 'All' button.  Maybe in the future add an id to the element to make the code a bit more readable. */
                    $('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]').trigger('click');


                }
                catch (err) {
                    console.error(err.message);
                }
            }); //end document.ready
        }

    } //end PageLoaded

// Source: HARLEY DAVIDSON (HD)_Phase 2_2436.cs
// PostSearchHistory(packages) // returns void
    this.PostSearchHistory = function(packages) {
        //debugger;
        for (let i = 0; i < packages.length; i++)
        {
            const currentDate = new Date();
            currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate());
            
            const shipDate = new Date(packages[i].Shipdate.Year,packages[i].Shipdate.Month-1,packages[i].Shipdate.Day);
            //alert(packages[i].Shipdate.Year + " | " + packages[i].Shipdate.Month + " | " + packages[i].Shipdate.Day)
            //alert(shipDate)
            
            const diffTime = Math.abs(shipDate - currentDate);
            const diffDays = Math.floor(diffTime / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)); 
            //console.log(diffTime + " milliseconds");
            //alert(diffDays + " days");
            if(diffDays > 30)
            {
                packages[i].CantPrint = true;
            }
        }
    }

// ViewCheckedLabels() // returns void
    function ViewCheckedLabels() {
        const batchItemArr = [];
        $('#tableBatchDetails').find('input[type=checkbox]:checked').each(function () {
            //debugger;
            console.log("Print");
            var btnPrint = $(this).closest('tr').find('input[type="button"][value="Print"]').first().trigger('click');
            batchItemArr.push($(this).attr('data'))
        });
        var dataObject = {};
        dataObject.Action = "RemoveBatchItem";
        let bLen = batchItemArr.length;
        for (let i = 0; i < bLen; i++) {
            if (i == 0) {
                dataObject.Content = batchItemArr[i];
            } else {
                dataObject.Content += "," + batchItemArr[i];
            }
        }
        var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(dataObject), UserContext: client.userContext };
        //debugger;
        clientService.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false)
    }

this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {

            type: "GET",
            url: "api/usercontext/GET",

            cache: false,
            success: function (result) {
                debugger;

            },
            error: function (jqXhr, exception) {

            }
        });

            type: "POST",
            url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            dataType: "json",           
            data: { UserContext: clientContext , "Data": nameaddress.Country},

				resp = JSON.parse(resp);
				if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
				{

					alert('No available Importer of Records');
				}
            },
            error: function (xhr) {
                debugger;
                alert(xhr.responseText);
            }
        });

// Source: ICON Clinical Research (PRAInternational)_PRA Intl Business Rules_1574.cs
// function PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) // returns undefined
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) {
        debugger;
        if (addressName !== '' && addressName !== 'ThirdPartyBillingAddress') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if (($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().length > 0) && ($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().length > 0)) {

                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    /* The values are stored in the format of 'string:CC'.  We only want the CC. */
                    var shipToCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().replace('string:', '');
                    var shipFromCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().replace('string:', '');

                    /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
                    if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
                        /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
                        SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                    }
                    else {
                        /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
                        if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                            SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                        }

                        //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
                    }
                } /* if ($('div.modal-dialog.modal-md:visible') */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */
        }
    };

// function EmailNotificationAddress(event) // returns undefined
    this.EmailNotificationAddress = function (event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];
        debugger;
        // if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
        //     SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
        //     SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // } else {
        //     SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // }

        if (ngModelName == 'ShipNotificationEmail') {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName == 'DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail') {
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName == 'DeliveryNotificationEmail') {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    };

// authorizationToken() // returns an authorization header object or undefined
authorizationToken: function () {
            debugger;

// userContext() // returns the user context response JSON
userContext: function () {
            debugger;
            var userContextUrl = 'api/usercontext/GET';
            var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            if (shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http')) {
                var url = new URL(shipExecServiceUrl);
                userContextUrl = url.origin + '/' + userContextUrl;
            }
            var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
            return $.get({url: userContextUrl, headers: authorizationToken, async: false}).responseJSON;
        }()

// BatchManager() // returns nothing
this.BatchManager = function() {
        debugger;

        // set user email
        var userEmail = $("div.navbar-collapse").text();
        userEmail = userEmail.match(/([a-zA-Z0-9._-]+@[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+\.[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+)/gi).toString();
        $("#email").val(userEmail);
        $("#email").change();

        IPSUploadFile();

        function IPSUploadFile() {
            $('body').delegate('#ipsUploadFile', 'click', function () {
                alertMessage('info', "Rate Process Started, an email will be sent upon completion");
                showSpinner();
                var vm = $(this).attr('vm')
                if (ensureLoadIPS(vm)) {
                    var fileName = cbr.loadIPS.file.name.split('.')[0];
                    debugger;
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.readAsDataURL(cbr.loadIPS.file);
                    reader.onload = function () {
                        var data = {
                            'UserContext': cbr.userContext,
                            'Data' : JSON.stringify({
                                'Action': 'Rate',
                                'Shipper': cbr.loadIPS.shipper,
                                'ShipDate': cbr.loadIPS.shipDate,
                                'Email': cbr.loadIPS.email,
                                'FileName': fileName,
                                'EncodedFile': this.result.split(',')[1],
                            })
                        }

                        $.post({ 
                            url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
                            data,
                            headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
                        }).done(function (result) {
                            hideSpinner();
                            if (result.ErrorCode > 0) {
                                alertMessage('danger', response.ErrorMessage);
                            } else {
                                alertMessage('success', "Rate Completed");
                                loadIPSReset();
                            }
                        }).fail(function (err) {
                            hideSpinner();
                            alertMessage('danger',"The process is taking longer than usual to complete but will continue to run on the server until the rate file is complete");
                        });	
                    }
                }
                // hide the spinner after 15 seconds
                setTimeout(function(){
                    hideSpinner();
                }, 15000);
            });
        }

        function loadIPSReset() {
            $.each( cbr.loadIPS, function(name, value){
                $('[ng-model="vm.loadIPS.' + name + '"]').val(null);
            });
        }

        function ensureLoadIPS(vm) {
            var msg = [];
            var result = true;

            if (vm == '') {
                msg.push('Please update all options and try again.');
            } else {
                cbr.loadIPS = JSON.parse(vm);
                //if (cbr.loadIPS.type == undefined) msg.push('\u2022Select Rate or Address Validation radio button.');
                if (cbr.loadIPS.shipper == undefined) msg.push('\u2022Missing Shipper.');
                if (cbr.loadIPS.shipDate == undefined) msg.push("\u2022Missing Ship Date.");
                if (cbr.loadIPS.email == undefined) {
                    msg.push('\u2022Missing Email Address.');
                } else {
                    if (invalidEmailAddress(cbr.loadIPS.email)) msg.push('\u2022Email Address is invalid.')
                }

                var files = $('#ipsFileInputField').prop('files');
                if (files.length == 0) {
                    msg.push('\u2022Missing File.')
                } else {
                    cbr.loadIPS.file = files[0];
                }
            }

            if (msg.length > 0) {
                result = false;
                alertMessage('danger', msg.join("<br />"));
                hideSpinner();
            }
            
            return result;
        }
    }

        function testbutton() {
            $('body').delegate('#buttonExportCODFile', 'click', function () {
                debugger;
                var shipper = $(this).attr('shipper');
                var carrier = $(this).attr('carrier');
                var historyId = $(this).attr('historyId');
                var historyShipDateYear = $(this).attr('shipDateYear');
                var historyShipDateMonth = $(this).attr('shipDateMonth');
                var historyShipDateDay = $(this).attr('shipDateDay');
                var isSftpChecked = $('#SftprBtnId').prop('checked');
                var isLocalChecked = $('#LocalrBtnId').prop('checked');
                debugger;

                // Send data to user method on the server side
                var usermethodParams = { "action": 1, "usercontext": client.userContext, "shipper": shipper, "historyId": historyId, "historyShipDateYear": historyShipDateYear, "historyShipDateMonth": historyShipDateMonth, "historyShipDateDay": historyShipDateDay, "carrier": carrier, "sftpSelectrdStatus": isSftpChecked, "localSelectrdStatus": isLocalChecked };
                var codFileString;

                var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
                
                clientService.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
                    debugger;                  

                    //****New code 01.24.2022****
                    var jsonString = $("<textarea/>").html(response.Data).text();

                    if (jsonString && isLocalChecked) {                        
                        codFileString = jsonString;

                        var data = new Blob([codFileString], { type: 'text/plain' });

                        var ie = navigator.userAgent.match(/MSIE\s([\d.]+)/),
                            ie11 = navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident\/7.0/) && navigator.userAgent.match(/rv:11/),
                            ieEdge = navigator.userAgent.match(/Edge/g),
                            ieVer = (ie ? ie[1] : (ie11 ? 11 : (ieEdge ? 12 : -1)));

                        // set the export file name 
                        var exportFileName = "ShipmentRequest" + historyShipDateYear + historyShipDateMonth + historyShipDateDay + "_1_" + shipper + ".txt"

                        if (ieVer > -1) {
                            window.navigator.msSaveBlob(codFileString, exportFileName);

                        } else {
                            var downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
                            downloadLink.download = exportFileName;
                            downloadLink.href = window.URL.createObjectURL(data);
                            downloadLink.style.display = "none";
                            document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                            downloadLink.click();
                            document.body.removeChild(link);
                        }
                    }
                });          
            })
        }
    }

// Source: L9 Sports (L9SPORTS)_L9 Client Rules_1694.cs
// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    //debugger;
    loadValue = loadValue.replace('!!', '');

    if (typeof shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== 'undefined' && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5.length > 2)
    {
      alertMessage('danger', shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5);
    }

    this.vm.getWeight();
    //$("#overrideRateShopping_Y").prop("checked", true);

    // Warn user if expedited service selected and PO box is checked
    const expServices = "UPS.NDA,UPS.2AM,UPS.2DA,UPS.EXP,USPS.PRIORITY,USPS.EXPR".split(',');

    let hasExpedited = expServices.some(service => shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol.includes(service));
    if (hasExpedited && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PoBox)
    {
      alertMessage('warning', "Order " + loadValue + " has an Expedited service selected but a PO box was used. Contact Customer Service for a new address.")
    }

    // if Int'l shipment, show Assign Commodities button, hide Add Package button group, and init AssignGoods
    //sna6dxb - 09-23-2022
    //don't need this any longer, the button is hidden by default in the template
    //$('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country !== "US")
    {
      $('#btnAssignCommodities').show();
      $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().hide();
      const Goods = new AssignGoods(this.vm);
    }
    else {
        // ensure Assign Commodities button is hidden in case they load an Int'l order by mistake, then load domestic
        $('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
        $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().show();
    }
  }

// ShowAssignGoodsPane() // returns void
  ShowAssignGoodsPane()
  {
    let that = this;
    //get rid of any previous entries
    $('#listItemContainer li:gt(0)').remove();

    //change the column width to make the descriptions longer
    //change this back when the user clicks the 'Apply' button
    $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6')

    //set a reference to the packages object as well as the commodities objects
    this.packages = this.viewModel.currentShipment.Packages;

    //get all the commodities in the shipment from all packages
    this.goods = $(this.packages).map(function(x, y)
    {
      return y.CommodityContents;
    });

    //loop the goods array and update the markup within the slideout panel
    $(this.goods).each(function(a, b)
    {
      //debugger;
      let k = 'e' + (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
      b.GoodsKey = k;

      if (b.packageIndex === undefined) {
        // initial index is undefined after loading order, default to fix NaN bug later
        b.packageIndex = 0;
      }
      //copy the source element
      let item = $('#liClone').clone(true).attr({ 'hash-key': b.$$hashKey, 'goods-key': b.GoodsKey, 'pkg-index': b.packageIndex }).removeAttr('id');

      //the customer is sending amounts that have sometimes 10 digits after the decimal point which is throwing exceptions when trying
      //to parseFloat so this is the simplest way to get around that.
      let cost = Math.round(b.UnitValue.Amount * 100) / 100;

      $(item).find('.goods-description').text(b.Description);
      $(item).find('.goods-quantity').html('(<strong>' + b.Quantity + '</strong>');
      $(item).find('.goods-unit-of-measure').text(b.QuantityUnitMeasure + ', ');
      $(item).find('.goods-declared-value').html('<strong>$' + cost + '</strong> ' + b.UnitValue.Currency + ')');
      $(item).find('.pkg-index-text').text(+(b.packageIndex) + 1);
      $(item).find('.header-logo').show();

      //append it to our list
      $('#divAssignCommodities ul.list-group').append(item);

      //show it gracefully
      $(item).show();

    });

    //create a working array object so we can manipulate the data non-destructively
    this.working = $.makeArray(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(this.goods)));

    $('#divAssignCommodities').show().animate({ left: 0 }, 400);
    $('.assign-to-pkg:visible').first().focus();
  }

// InitiateDelegates() // returns void
  InitiateDelegates()
  {
    let that = this

    $('body').delegate('#btnApplyCommodityAssignments', 'click', function(e)
    {
      that.ApplyCommodityAssignments();
    });

    $('body').delegate('.btn-show-split-form', 'click', function(e)
    {
      let div = $(this).closest('div').find('.split-pkgs-modal').first();
      $(div).tooltip({ container: 'body' });

      $(div).css('display', 'flex').fadeIn();
      $('.split-pkgs-modal:visible').find('input').first().focus();

      //hide the split button now...and the input
      $(this).hide();
      $(this).closest('div').find('.assign-to-pkg').hide();
    });

    $('body').delegate('input.btn-go-split-pkgs', 'click', function(e)
    {
      console.log('btn-go-split-pkgs click event handler');

      let li = $(this).closest('li').first();
      let div = $(this).closest('div').first();

      $(li).find('.pkg-index-text').first().text('1');

      //val - 1 as the first entry will be the first package
      let v = $(div).find('input[type=number]').first().val();

      that.UpdateGoodsObject(v, li);

      $('.split-pkgs-modal').hide();
    });

    $('body').delegate('#btnCancelAssignGoods', 'click', function(e)
    {
      that.HideAssignGoodsPane();
    });

    //if the user escapes out of the split modal, hide the modal and show the previous forms
    $('body').delegate('.split-pkgs-modal', 'keydown', function(e)
    {
      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      if (keycode === 27)
      {
        //need to show the previous input and button now
        let li = $(this).closest('li');

        that.CancelSplitOfPackages(li);
      }
    });

    //if the user presses enter or tab in the num-of-items number input, move to the next one
    //these are the number inputs after the items have been split across packages
    $('body').delegate('.num-of-items-in-pkg', 'keydown focusout', function(e)
    {
      console.log('.num-of-items-in-pkg keydown focusout event handler');

      $('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip('hide');

      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      if (keycode === 13 || keycode === 9)
      {
        //disable the input, update the commodity object, focus on the next box input
        //$(this).closest('div').find('.assign-to-pkg').focus();
        that.UpdateListItemPackageQuantities($(this).closest('li'));
      }
    });

    //user hits enter in the input box, click the button for them
    $('body').delegate('.num-of-pkgs-to-use', 'keyup keydown', function(e)
    {
      console.log('.num-of-pkgs-to-use keyup keydown event handler');
      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      let btn = $(this).closest('div:visible').find('input.btn-go-split-pkgs');

      $(btn).attr('disabled', $(this).val() < 2);

      if (keycode == 13) //enter
      {
        //let btn = $(this).closest('div:visible').find('input.btn-go-split-pkgs');
        $(btn).trigger('click');
      }
    });

    //this was formerly .scan-input.  as of 9/24/2022, removing the split functionality completely
    //with this change, only need to get the numerical value out of the input
    $('body').delegate('.assign-to-pkg', 'keydown focusout', function(e)
    {
      console.log('.assign-to-pkg keydown focusout event handler');
      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      debugger;
      if (keycode == 13 || keycode == 9 || e.type == "focusout") //enter
      {
        e.preventDefault();
        //pull only the number from whatever was passed.  make sure it is greater than 0 since we can't assign a good a pkg zero.
        const val = $(this).val().replace(/[^1-9]/g, '');

        let li = $(this).closest('li');
        
        if (val)
        {
          //console.log('assigning this to ', val);
          //assign the integer to the line item header (not shown, but may be shown in the future)
          //this one is easy, just assign the pkg-index attr to whatever they scanned.  when the apply button is clicked it will assign the commodities
          //let li = $(this).closest('li');
          $(li).find('.pkg-index-text').first().text(val);
          $(li).find('button').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
          $(li).attr('pkg-index', val - 1);
          $(li).attr('pkg-status', 'packed');

          //find the matching item in the this.working array and update the package index
          let item = $.grep(that.working, function(good, i) { return good.$$hashKey == $(li).attr('hash-key') })[0];
          item.packageIndex = val - 1;
          //return;
        }
        // set focus to next li input box
        if (e.type !== "focusout") {
          $(li).next().find('.assign-to-pkg').focus().change();
        }
      }
    });

    $('#btnAssignCommodities').on('click', function(e)
    {
      if ($('#divAssignCommodities').is(':visible')) return;
      that.ShowAssignGoodsPane();
    });
  }

// GetEmail() // returns the extracted email text as a string
   GetEmail(){
      var emailText = "";
      var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a"); 
      Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag){
         if(tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!","").trim(); 
      });
      return emailText;
   }

// function getCostCenterReport(element) // returns jQuery.Promise
function getCostCenterReport(element) {
    debugger;
    var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
    var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
    var context = client.userContext;
    var costcenter = $(element).attr('data-costcenter');
    if (costcenter) {
        var searchCriteria = { DateStart: $('input[ng-model="vm.dtstart"]').val(), DateEnd: $('input[ng-model="vm.dtend"]').val(), CostCenter: costcenter };
        var data = { Action: element.id, Content: JSON.stringify(searchCriteria) };
       return $.post({ url:shipExecServiceUrl +'/UserMethod',
              data: {UserContext: userContext, Data:JSON.stringify(data)}, headers: authorizationToken},
            function (response, status, xhr) {
                downloadFile(costcenter, response["Data"]);
            }
        ).done(function () {
        });
    }
}

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        debugger;

        var i = 0, len = shipmentRequest.Packages.length;
        for (; i < len; i++) {
            var currentPackage = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
            debugger;
            if (currentPackage == null
                || currentPackage.CommodityContents == null
                || currentPackage.CommodityContents.length == 0) {
                var errorMsg = 'To obtain a UPS label to ship you must go to the Goods Tab above and process a paperless invoice for this shipment. Instructions on how to do this are located in your Starterpack.'
                console.log(errorMsg);
                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMsg);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
                throw Error(errorMsg);
            }
        }

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods');
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModal');
    }

        // $('#Maxlabel').val('1');
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {


        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;


        if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
        }

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

        //Storing StudyReference codes on the Miscreference17
        var studyReferenceCode = null;
        var studyReferenceCodeList = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations.length; i++) {
            debugger;
            studyReferenceCode = this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations[i].Value.split(',').map(x => x.trim());
            studyReferenceCodeList.push(studyReferenceCode);
        }
        var shipper = null;
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $("#OK").on("click", function () {
                debugger;
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val().trim();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if (arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)) {
                    var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue);
                    var selectedStudy = arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                    var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                    var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();

                    debugger;
                    var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                    var selectedSite = arrayOrders2[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();

                    //Assigning Shipper based on StudyReferenceCode available on validation list
                    for (var j = 0; j < studyReferenceCodeList.length; j++) {
                        var firstCode = studyReferenceCodeList[j];
                        if (firstCode.length >= 2 && firstCode[0] == selectedValue) {
                            shipper = "string:" + firstCode[1];
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(shipper);
                            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];


                        }
                    }

                }
                else {
                    alert("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                    throw new Error("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                }

                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                //GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest);

                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();

            });

        });

        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

    }

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods');
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModal');

        //If the user profile is EU to UK, then Pickup LatestTimeReady can be calculated.
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 == "2") {

            //Storing the Number of Maximum labels in Misc Referene14.
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 = $('#Maxlabel').val();

            //Validating the maximum label count.
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == "" || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 % 1 !== 0) {
                alert("Maximum label count is invalid");
                throw new Error("Maximum label count is invalid");
            }
            else if (!(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 >= 1 && shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 <= 25)) {
                throw new Error("Number of labels needs to be a valid number between 1 and 25.");
            }
            
        }

    }

this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        debugger;
        
       
        var i = 0, len = shipmentRequest.Packages.length;
        for (; i < len; i++) {
            var currentPackage = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
            debugger;
            if (currentPackage == null
                || currentPackage.CommodityContents == null
                || currentPackage.CommodityContents.length == 0) {
                var errorMsg = 'To obtain a UPS label to ship you must go to the Goods Tab above and process a paperless invoice for this shipment. Instructions on how to do this are located in your Starterpack.'
                console.log(errorMsg);
                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMsg);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
                throw Error(errorMsg);
            }
        }

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods');
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModal');
    }

// function setResponseLabel(responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) // returns void
this.setResponseLabel = function (responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
        console.log("Upload Response: " + result);

        var label = $('#' + responseLabelId);
        if (label) {

            //debugger;

            if (sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + sessionStorageErrorFileName
                    + " - document exceeds maximum size (1.0 MB)";

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }

            else if (!result.Success) {
                // If the call is not successful, display an error message in a modal
                //debugger;
                var existingMessage = $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html();

                // Creates the error message
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + result.FileName
                    + " during Leg "
                    + result.Leg
                    + ".";

                // If there is an existing error message, append to it
                if (existingMessage && existingMessage.length > 0) {
                    errorMessage = existingMessage + '<br /><br />' + errorMessage;
                }

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }
        }
    }

// function convertFileInputToBase64(inputId, leg) // returns Promise<object | undefined>
this.convertFileInputToBase64 = function (inputId, leg) {
        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {

            var data = {};
            const fileInput = $('#' + inputId);

            // Do not continue if there are no files
            if (!fileInput ||
                fileInput.length === 0 ||
                !fileInput[0].files ||
                fileInput[0].files.length === 0) {
                return;
            }

            // Get basic file info
            var file = fileInput[0].files[0];
            var fileName = file.name;

            // Create reader for reading files
            var reader = new FileReader();
            reader.readAsDataURL(file);
            reader.addEventListener("load", function () {

                // Create and return payload for upload call
                data = {
                    Action: "PaperlessDocUpload",
                    FileName: fileName,
                    encodedString: reader.result.split(',')[1],
                    shipperName: that.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper,
                    leg: leg
                }

                resolve(data);

            }, false);

            reader.addEventListener("error", function (error) {
                reject(error);
            }, false);

        });

    }

// function setCommodityDelegate() // returns void
function setCommodityDelegate() {
        checkElmLoaded('[name="commoditiesModalForm"]').then((elm) => {
            debugger;
            const parentElm = elm;
            if (elm) {
                debugger;
                var footer = elm.querySelector('.modal-footer');
                if (footer) {
                    var saveButton = footer.querySelector('[value="Save"]');
                    if (saveButton) {
                        saveButton.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                            debugger;
                            var form = e.target.parentElement.parentElement;
                            var quantityUOM = form.querySelector('[ng-model="vm.commodityContent.QuantityUnitMeasure"]');
                            if (quantityUOM && quantityUOM.options) {
                                console.log('clicked');
                                var optionArray = Array.from(quantityUOM.options);

                                if (optionArray && optionArray.length > 0)
                                    var eachOption = optionArray.filter((x) => x.value == 'string:EA');
                                console.log('eachOption');
                                console.log(eachOption);
                                if (eachOption && eachOption.length == 1) {
                                    var indexOfEAOption = optionArray.indexOf(eachOption[0]);
                                    if (indexOfEAOption > 0) {
                                        quantityUOM.selectedIndex = indexOfEAOption;
                                        console.log('index');
                                        console.log(indexOfEAOption);
                                        quantityUOM.dispatchEvent(new window.Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                                        console.log('dispatched');
                                    }
                                }

                                debugger;
                                setTimeout(setCommodityDelegate, 500);
                            }

                            //that.vm.commodityContent.QuantityUnitMeasure = 'EA';
                        })
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

// function setUploadDelegates() // returns void
function setUploadDelegates() {

        debugger;
        setCommodityDelegate();

        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfModal', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfModalClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 'change');

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click', function (e) {

            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "true";

            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput[0].value = null;
            }
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";

            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            //debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', '');

            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
                if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                    uploadSuccessLabel.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    debugger;
                    that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                    $('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear').click();
                }
                else {

                    //debugger;
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 1, e).then(function (ret, e) {
                        //debugger;
                        //that.currentShipment.MiscReference19 = JSON.stringify(ret);
                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            //var test = this.setResponseLabel;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                            //debugger;
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfModal', 'click', function (e) {
            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfModalClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsModalInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsModalInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsModalInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsModalInput[0].value = null;
            }
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = "false";
            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', '');
            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabelModal = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');
                if (uploadSuccessLabelModal) {
                    uploadSuccessLabelModal.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    var test2 = that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                }
                else {
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 2).then(function (ret) {
                        //debugger;

                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName'));
                            //debugger;
                        }


                    });
                }
            }
        });

    }

            InitElements: function (LogToServer) {
                debugger;
                $('div.top-tool-bar > div.pull-left').prepend($('<button />').addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary').attr('id', 'LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').text('StudyReferenceCodes').fadeIn());
                /* Set up all delegates from within this block. */

                    StudyReferenceCodeModal.LoadStudyReferenceCodeDialog();
                });

                $('body').delegate('#buttonCloseLoadWithoutSaving', 'click', function (e) {
                    StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
                });
            }

// PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
this.PostShip = function (shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        debugger;
        this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference; //Study Reference code

        this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;  //Protocol Number

        this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;  //Site Number

        $('#Maxlabel').val('1');
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
        }

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

        //Storing StudyReference codes on the Miscreference17
        var studyReferenceCode = null;
        var studyReferenceCodeList = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations.length; i++) {
            debugger;
            studyReferenceCode = this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations[i].Value.split(',').map(x => x.trim());
            studyReferenceCodeList.push(studyReferenceCode);
        }
        var shipper = null;
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $("#OK").on("click", function () {
                debugger;
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val().trim();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if (arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)) {
                    var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue);
                    var selectedStudy = arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                    var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                    var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();

                    var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                    var selectedSite = arrayOrders2[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();

                    //Assigning Shipper based on StudyReferenceCode available on validation list
                    for (var j = 0; j < studyReferenceCodeList.length; j++) {
                        var firstCode = studyReferenceCodeList[j];
                        if (firstCode.length >= 2 && firstCode[0] == selectedValue) {
                            shipper = "string:" + firstCode[1];
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(shipper);
                            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];


                        }
                    }

                }
                else {
                    alert("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                    throw new Error("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                }

                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                //GetUserShipper(selectedStudy,shipmentRequest);

                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();

            });

        });

        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

    }

// GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest) // returns void
function GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest) {
        var jsonData;
        var dataObject = {
            StudyReferenceCode: selectedStudy,
            UserContext: client.userContext
        };

        var payload = JSON.stringify(dataObject);
        debugger;
        var data = { Data: payload, UserContext: client.userContext };

        var ajaxRequest = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, true);

        ajaxRequest.done(function (data) {

            jsonData = data.Data;
            console.log(jsonData);
            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(jsonData);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];

        });

    }

                debugger;

                /* Set up all delegates from within this block. */
                $('body').delegate('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData', 'click', function (e) {
                    StudyReferenceCodeModal.LoadStudyReferenceCodeDialog();
                });

                $('body').delegate('#buttonCloseLoadWithoutSaving', 'click', function (e) {
                    StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
                });
            }
