// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //debugger;
        if (this.vm.profile.Name == "Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile") {
            //Setting Leg2 Company
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 == '') {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[3].Value;
            }

            //Setting Leg2 Shipper
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;
        }

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods');
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModal');
    }

// function PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
this.PostShip = function (shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        //debugger;
        $('#Leg2LabelRequired').prop('checked', false);
        $('#DryIceRequired').prop('checked', false);
        $('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').prop('checked', false);
        $('#Leg2PackageWeight').val('');
        $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').val('');
        $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
        $('#quantity').val('');
        $('#EmptyPackaging').prop('checked', false);
        $('#displayMessage').hide();

        // Clear the upload error modal text
        $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html('');

        var userData1 = shipmentResponse.Packages[0].UserData1;
        var userData2 = shipmentResponse.Packages[0].UserData2;

        if (userData1) {
            var result = JSON.parse(userData1.replace(/'/g, '"'));
            //debugger;
            this.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', result);
        }

        if (userData2) {
            var result = JSON.parse(userData2.replace(/'/g, '"'));
            //debugger;
            this.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', result);
        }

    }

// function setResponseLabel(responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) // returns void
this.setResponseLabel = function (responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
        console.log("Upload Response: " + result);

        var label = $('#' + responseLabelId);
        if (label) {

            //debugger;

            if (sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + sessionStorageErrorFileName
                    + " - document exceeds maximum size (1.0 MB)";

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }

            else if (!result.Success) {
                // If the call is not successful, display an error message in a modal
                //debugger;
                var existingMessage = $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html();

                // Creates the error message
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + result.FileName
                    + " during Leg "
                    + result.Leg
                    + ".";

                // If there is an existing error message, append to it
                if (existingMessage && existingMessage.length > 0) {
                    errorMessage = existingMessage + '<br /><br />' + errorMessage;
                }

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }
        }
    }

// function PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        this.clearSessionState();
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;
        that.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;
    }

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;

        //Declaring variables.
        var custom1_values, custom1, custom2, custom3, custom4, custom5, custom6, customData;
        var customValues = {};
        var customKeysArray = [];
        var CustomData_AfterCustom4 = [];
        var item;

        customData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
        // Iterate over the CustomData array and map values to their respective keys
        $.each(customData, function (index, item) {
            customValues[item.Key] = item.Value;
        });

        if (this.vm.profile.Name == 'Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile') {
            for (var i in customData.length) {
                item = customData[i];
                customKeysArray.push(item.Key);
            }

            var startIndex = -1;
            // Find the index of the key "Custom5"
            for (var i = 0; i < customData.length; i++) {
                if (customData[i].Key === "Custom5") {
                    startIndex = i;
                    break;
                }
            }

            // If "Custom5" is found, start storing values from it onwards
            if (startIndex !== -1) {
                for (var j = startIndex; j < customData.length; j++) {
                    CustomData_AfterCustom4.push(customData[j].Value);
                }
            }

            // Now, customValues object contains all custom values accessible by their keys
            var custom1 = customValues['Custom1'];
            var custom2 = customValues['Custom2'];
            var custom3 = customValues['Custom3'];
            var custom4 = customValues['Custom4'];
            var custom5 = customValues['Custom5'];
            var custom6 = customValues['Custom6'];
        } else {
            //debugger;
            custom1 = customValues['Custom1'];
            custom2 = customValues['Custom2'];
        }

        //Checking DryIceRequired sets true via User Custom1 data.
        if (custom1.split(',').length > 1) {
            custom1_values = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom1, ',');
        } else {
            throw new Error("Custom1 is not Comma delimited string.");
        }

        //Setting the Leg1Shipper
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = custom1_values[0];

        //Creating Dry Ice Required Checkbox
        if ($('#DryIceRequired').length == 0 && custom1_values[1] == "true") {
            //Adding DryIceRequired checkbox and its label.
            $('div.col-md-6:last').append($('<input />', {
                type: 'checkbox',
                id: 'DryIceRequired',
                name: 'DryIceRequired'
            }));
            $('div.col-md-6:last').append($('<label />', {
                for: 'DryIceRequired',
                text: 'Dry Ice Required'
            }));
        }

        //Comparing the User Custom2 with the Profile enabled Services and remove the unmatched services from the Service UI.
        var arrayValues_custom2;
        if (custom2 != null || custom2 != undefined) {
            arrayValues_custom2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom2, ',');
            var matchedValues = [];
            var profileServices = this.vm.profile.Services;
            profileServices.forEach(function (value1) {
                var serviceExists = arrayValues_custom2.some(function (value) {
                    return value1.Name.indexOf(value) !== -1;
                });
                if (serviceExists) {
                    matchedValues.push(value1);
                }
            });

            //Populating the Matched services on the Service UI.
            $(document).ready(function () {
                var mySelect = $('select[multiple="multiple"][property="Service"]');
                mySelect.empty(); //Clearing the existing Services listed out in the Service UI list.

                for (var i in matchedValues) {
                    mySelect.append($('<option></option>').attr('value', matchedValues[i].Symbol).text(matchedValues[i].Name));

                }
            });
        }

        //Retrieving Custom Data values after CustomData4(Leg2 Companies).
        var CustomDataCount = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData.length;

        var CustomData_FirstValues = []; //Fetch the First strings from Customdata after Custom4.
        var CustomData_OtherValues = []; //Fetch the rest of other strings from Customdata after Custom4.

        // Loop through each inner array in CustomData_AfterCustom4
        for (var i = 0; i < CustomData_AfterCustom4.length; i++) {

            var customData = CustomData_AfterCustom4[i];

            //var customData_values = customData.Value;

            var valuesArray = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(customData, ',');

            var firstValue = valuesArray.shift().trim();

            //Store the first string from the Custom data.
            CustomData_FirstValues.push(firstValue);

            //Store the remaining values
            CustomData_OtherValues.push(valuesArray.map(val => val.trim()));
        }


        //debugger;
        //Enabling the MiscReference1 field based on Profile.
        if (this.vm.profile.Name == "Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile") {

           // debugger;

            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide(); //When page loaded, MISCREFERENCE1 will be hidden.
                $('body').delegate('#DryIceRequired', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#DryIceRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        //debugger;
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').show();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "true";
                    } else {
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "false";
                    }
                });
            });

            $(document).ready(function () {
                if (custom1_values[2] == "true") {
                    $('#EmptyPackaging').hide();
                    $('label[for="EmptyPackaging"]').hide();
                }
                else {
                    $('#EmptyPackaging').show();
                    $('label[for="EmptyPackaging"]').show();
                }

            });

            //Creating Central Labs Frozen Sample Return Checkbox
            if ($('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').length == 0 && custom1_values[2] == "true") {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').addClass('inline-checkbox').append(
                    $('<input />').addClass('checkbox').attr({
                        'type': 'checkbox',
                        'id': 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn',
                        'name': 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn'
                    }),
                    $('<label />').attr('for', 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').text('Central Labs Frozen Samples Return')
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);

            }
            else {
                //Creating Empty Packaging Checkbox
                if ($('#EmptyPackaging').length == 0) {
                    //debugger;
                    var checkboxAndLabelContainer_Empty = $('<div>').addClass('inline-checkbox').append(
                        $('<input />').addClass('checkbox').attr({
                            'type': 'checkbox',
                            'id': 'EmptyPackaging',
                            'name': 'EmptyPackaging'
                        }),
                        $('<label />').attr('for', 'EmptyPackaging').text('Empty Packaging')
                    );

                    $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer_Empty);

                }



                //Setting MiscReference7 to true if Empty Packaging Checkbox is checked.
                $('body').delegate('#EmptyPackaging', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#EmptyPackaging').is(':checked')) {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = "true";
                    } else {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = "false";
                    }
                });
            }


            //Setting Leg2 Dry Ice weight hidden by default
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
                $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').hide();
            });
            //Setting MiscReference7 to true if Central Labs Frozen Sample Return Checkbox is checked.
            $('body').delegate('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn', 'change', function (e) {
                if ($('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').is(':checked')) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = "true";

                    $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').show();
                    $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').show();

                } else {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = "false";
                    $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
                    $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').hide();
                }
            });

            //Creating Leg2 Dry Ice Weight
            if ($('#Leg2DryIceWeight').length == 0) {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').append(
                    $('<label />').attr({
                        'for': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;top:120px;width:160px;'

                    }).text('Dry Ice Weight'),
                    $('<input />').attr({
                        'type': 'text',
                        'id': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'name': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;border:1px solid black;top:140px;width:160px;'
                    }),
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);
            }

            //Setting MiscReference10 to true if Leg2 Dry Ice Weight is present.
            $('body').delegate('#Leg2DryIceWeight', 'change', function (e) {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference10 = $(this).val();
            });
            //Creating Leg2 Package Weight
            if ($('#Leg2PackageWeight').length == 0) {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').append(
                    $('<label />').attr({
                        'for': 'Leg2PackageWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;top:70px;width:160px;'

                    }).text('Package Weight'),
                    $('<input />').attr({
                        'type': 'text',
                        'id': 'Leg2PackageWeight',
                        'name': 'Leg2PackageWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;border:1px solid black;top:90px;width:160px;'
                    }),
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);
            }
            //debugger;
            //Setting MiscReference9 to true if Leg2 Package Weight is present.
            $('body').delegate('#Leg2PackageWeight', 'change', function (e) {
                //debugger;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference9 = $(this).val();
            });

            $('#divModalCompanyPopup').delegate('#Leg2PackageWeight', 'change', function (e) {
                //debugger;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference9 = $(this).val();
            });

            //Manual Upload
            var commodityLists = GetCommodityContents();
            $.each(commodityLists.CommodityContents, function (index, option) {
                var textMessage = commodityLists.CommodityContents[index].Description + ' ' + commodityLists.CommodityContents[index].HarmonizedCode;

                $('#commodityKey').append($('<option>', {
                    value: JSON.stringify(option),
                    text: textMessage
                }));
            });

            $('#addButton').one('click', function () {

                var showMessage = $('<div>').attr('id', 'displayMessage').text("Commodity added").css('font-weight', 'bold');
                $('.manualUpload').after(showMessage);

                var quantity = $('#quantity').val();
                if (quantity % 1 !== 0) {
                    alert("Qty is invalid");
                }
                else {
                    //Store Quantity in MiscReference15
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference15 = quantity;
                }

                //Store commodity content in Misc Reference14
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 = $('#commodityKey').val();
            });

            //Creating Service Dropdown if User Custom4 is present.
            var hasCustom4 = false;
            for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData.length; i++) {
                if (this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[i].Key === "Custom4") {
                    hasCustom4 = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (hasCustom4) {
                if (custom4 != '' && custom4 != 'undefined' && custom4 != null && $('#Service').length === 0) {
                    //Creating Service Dropdown menu.
                    var labelAndSelect1 = $('<label />').attr('for', 'Service').text('Service: ')
                        .add($('<select />').addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary').attr({
                            'id': 'Service',
                            'name': 'Service'
                        }).fadeIn());

                    $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend(labelAndSelect1);

                    var arrayOfValues_custom4 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom4, ',');

                    if (arrayOfValues_custom4.length > 1) {
                        $.each(arrayOfValues_custom4, function (i, e) {
                            $('#Service').append($('<option>', {
                                value: e,
                                text: e
                            }));
                        });

                        $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend($('<div />', {
                            'class': 'spacer'
                        }));

                    } else {
                        throw new Error("Custom4 is not comma-delimited.");
                    }
                }
            } else {
                alert("Custom4 is not present");
            }


            //Use case: 5 User Custom data fields -> Leg2 companies will be present only at the custom5 field.
            var CustomData5_FirstValues = [];
            var CustomData5_OtherValues = [];

            //if (CustomDataCount == 5) {
            //debugger;
            if ($('#Company').length === 0) {

                var custom5_Values = [];
                custom5_Values = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom5, ',');
                var custom5_firstValue = custom5_Values.shift().trim();

                //Store the first value
                CustomData5_FirstValues.push(custom5_firstValue);

                // Store the remaining values
                CustomData5_OtherValues.push(custom5_Values.map(val => val.trim()));
                //debugger;
                $('#CompanyName').val(custom5_Values[0]);
                $('#CompanyContact').val(custom5_Values[1]);
                $('#CompanyAddress').val(custom5_Values[2]);
                $('#CompanyCity').val(custom5_Values[3]);
                if (custom5_Values.Length > 7) {
                    //debugger;
                    $('#CompanyStateProvince').val(custom5_Values[4]);
                    $('#CompanyPostalCode').val(custom5_Values[5]);
                    $('#CompanyCountry').val(custom5_Values[6]);
                    $('#CompanyPhone').val(custom5_Values[7]);

                } else {
                    // debugger;
                    $('#CompanyStateProvince').val("");
                    $('#CompanyPostalCode').val(custom5_Values[4]);
                    $('#CompanyCountry').val(custom5_Values[5]);
                    $('#CompanyPhone').val(custom5_Values[6]);

                }

                $('body').delegate('#Leg2LabelRequired', 'change', this.vm, function (e) {
                    //debugger;
                    if ($('#Leg2LabelRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        //debugger;
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 = "true";
                        CompanyPopup.InitElements(function (selectedCompany, selectedService) {

                            //debugger;
                            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = CustomData5_OtherValues.toString();

                            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = selectedService;

                        });
                    }
                });
            }


            if ($('#Company').length === 0) {

                if ((custom5 != '' && custom5 != 'undefined' && custom5 != null) && (custom6 != '' && custom6 != 'undefined' && custom6 != null)) {
                    //Creating Company Dropdown menu.
                    var labelAndSelect = $('<label />').attr('for', 'Company').text('Company: ')
                        .add($('<select />').addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary').attr({
                            'id': 'Company',
                            'name': 'Company'
                        }).fadeIn());

                    //$('div.modal-body').prepend(labelAndSelect);
                    $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend(labelAndSelect);



                    $.each(CustomData_FirstValues, function (i, e) {
                        $('#Company').append($('<option>', {
                            value: e,
                            text: e
                        }));
                    });

                    $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend($('<div />', {
                        'class': 'spacer' // Ensure you define this class in your CSS with the desired spacing
                    }));

                    // Event listener for company selection change
                    $('body').delegate('#Company', 'change', function (e) {
                        //debugger;
                        var selectedCompany = $(this).find(":selected").val();
                        CompanyPopup.populateCorrespondingValues(selectedCompany, CustomData_FirstValues, CustomData_OtherValues);
                    });

                    // Trigger change event on company dropdown to populate corresponding values by default
                    $('#Company').trigger('change');

                }

                //If Leg2LabelRequired check box is checked, setting MiscReference6 to true and populating the Company and Service values on the Modal.
                $('body').delegate('#Leg2LabelRequired', 'change', this.vm, function (e) {
                    if ($('#Leg2LabelRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 = "true";

                        if ((custom4 != '' || custom4 != 'undefined' || custom4 != null) || (custom5 != '' || custom5 != 'undefined' || custom5 != null) && (custom6 != '' || custom6 != 'undefined' || custom6 != null)) {

                            CompanyPopup.InitElements(function (selectedCompany, selectedService) {

                                var com = CompanyPopup.populateCorrespondingValues(selectedCompany, CustomData_FirstValues, CustomData_OtherValues);

                                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = com.toString();
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = selectedService;

                            });
                            $("#buttonCompanyPopup").click();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }

            //debugger;
            //Setting Leg1 and Leg2 PDF Invoice default by False.         
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = "false";


        } else {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide(); //When page loaded, MISCREFERENCE1 will be hidden.
                $('body').delegate('#DryIceRequired', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#DryIceRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        //debugger;
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').show();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "true";

                    } else {
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "false";
                    }
                });
            });

            //Setting Leg1 PDF Invoice default by False
            //debugger;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";

        }
        //debugger;
        //Assigning the User address to Return Address
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;
        //this.vm.profile.Shippers= this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        //Assigning the Weight Units to "KG" if Ship From country is not US.
        //debugger;
        var selectedShipper = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper; //$('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val();
        var map = $.grep(this.vm.profile.Shippers, function (shipper) {
            console.log(shipper.Symbol);
            return shipper.Symbol == selectedShipper;
        })[0];
        if (map.Country != "US") {
            //debugger;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Units = "KG";
        }
        
        
         //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    
                     var total=0;
                for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                    total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                }
                var inst=[];
                inst.push(total);
                debugger;
				shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions=inst[0].toString();
               
                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });
        
    }

// function clearUploadMessages() // returns void
function clearUploadMessages() {

        var standardSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
        var modalSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');

        if (standardSuccessLabel) {
            standardSuccessLabel.text('No file selected');
        }

        if (modalSuccessLabel) {
            modalSuccessLabel.text('No file selected');
        }
    }

// function setUploadDelegates() // returns void
function setUploadDelegates() {

        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfModal', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfModalClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 'change');

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click', function (e) {
            //debugger;
            //that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "true";

            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput[0].value = null;
            }
            //debugger;
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";

            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            //debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', '');

            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
                if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                    uploadSuccessLabel.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                    $('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear').click();
                }
                else {
                    that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "true";
                    //debugger;
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 1, e).then(function (ret, e) {
                        //debugger;
                        //that.currentShipment.MiscReference19 = JSON.stringify(ret);
                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfModal', 'click', function (e) {
            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfModalClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsModalInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsModalInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsModalInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsModalInput[0].value = null;
            }
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = "false";
            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            //debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', '');
            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabelModal = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');
                if (uploadSuccessLabelModal) {
                    uploadSuccessLabelModal.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    var test2 = that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                    $('#btnUploadPdfModalClear').click();
                }
                else {
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 2).then(function (ret) {
                        //debugger;

                        that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = "true";

                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName'));
                            //debugger;
                        }



                    });
                }
            }
        });

    }

// function populateCorrespondingValues(selectedCompany, CustomData_FirstValues, CustomData_OtherValues) // returns correspondingValues
populateCorrespondingValues: function (selectedCompany, CustomData_FirstValues, CustomData_OtherValues) {


                var index = CustomData_FirstValues.indexOf(selectedCompany);
                if (index !== -1) {

                    correspondingValues = CustomData_OtherValues[index];
                    $('#CompanyName').val(correspondingValues[0]);
                    $('#CompanyContact').val(correspondingValues[1]);
                    $('#CompanyAddress').val(correspondingValues[2]);
                    $('#CompanyCity').val(correspondingValues[3]);
                    if (correspondingValues.length > 7) {
                        //debugger;
                        $('#CompanyStateProvince').val(correspondingValues[4]);
                        $('#CompanyPostalCode').val(correspondingValues[5]);
                        $('#CompanyCountry').val(correspondingValues[6]);
                        $('#CompanyPhone').val(correspondingValues[7]);
                    } else {
                        //debugger;
                        $('#CompanyStateProvince').val("");
                        $('#CompanyPostalCode').val(correspondingValues[4]);
                        $('#CompanyCountry').val(correspondingValues[5]);
                        $('#CompanyPhone').val(correspondingValues[6]);
                    }

                }
                return correspondingValues;

            }

// function CloseDialogWithoutSaving(selectedCompany, selectedService, callback) // returns void
CloseDialogWithoutSaving: function (selectedCompany, selectedService, callback) {

                $('#divModalCompanyPopup').hide();
                Tools.HideLoader();

                if (callback) {
                    callback(selectedCompany, selectedService);
                }

            }

// function HideLoader() // returns void
HideLoader: function () {
                //debugger;
                $('div.loading').removeClass('ng-show').addClass('ng-hide');
                this.HideOverlay();
            }

// function HideOverlay() // returns void
HideOverlay: function () {
                //debugger;
                $('div.overlay').hide();
            }

// function GetUniqueArrayFromString(inString, stringDelimiter = ',') // returns array
GetUniqueArrayFromString: function (inString, stringDelimiter = ',') {
                //debugger;
                var trimArray = $.grep(inString.split(stringDelimiter), function (a) {
                    return a.trim().length > 0;
                });
                /* Get rid of any duplicate array entries. */
                //trimArray = trimArray.filter((e, i, a) => a.indexOf(e) === i);
                return trimArray;
            }

// Source: MarkenLLP (MLLP)_Marken_Phase3_CBR_2501.cs
// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;

        $(document).on('click', '[ng-click="vm.ok()"]', function(){
       debugger;
       
           var total=0;
           var quan=0;
           var unitValue=0;
           var com= shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents;
           for(var item=0; item<com.length; item++){
               quan=com[item].Quantity;
               unitValue=com[item].UnitValue.Amount;
               total += parseFloat(quan)* parseFloat(unitValue);
           }
         
           $("#totalComm").text(total);
        });
    }

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
    this.AddPackage = function (shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
        debugger;
        var packageIndex = that.vm.packageIndex;
        if (packageIndex > 0) {
            var current = that.vm.currentShipment.Packages[packageIndex];
            var previous = that.vm.currentShipment.Packages[packageIndex - 1];
            current.WorldEaseCode = previous.WorldEaseCode
            current.InvoiceFreight.Amount = previous.InvoiceFreight.Amount;
        }
    }

// this.setResponseLabel(responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) // returns undefined
    this.setResponseLabel = function (responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
        debugger;
        console.log("Upload Response: " + result);

        var label = $('#' + responseLabelId);
        if (label) {

            //debugger;

            if (sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + sessionStorageErrorFileName
                    + " - document exceeds maximum size (1.0 MB)";

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }

            else if (!result.Success) {
                // If the call is not successful, display an error message in a modal
                //debugger;
                var existingMessage = $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html();

                // Creates the error message
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + result.FileName
                    + " during Leg "
                    + result.Leg
                    + ".";

                // If there is an existing error message, append to it
                if (existingMessage && existingMessage.length > 0) {
                    errorMessage = existingMessage + '<br /><br />' + errorMessage;
                }

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }
        }
    }

// GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    function GetUserShipper(selectedStudy,shipmentRequest) {
       var jsonData;
       var dataObject = {
                    StudyReferenceCode:selectedStudy, 
                    UserContext: client.userContext
                };
 
                var payload = JSON.stringify(dataObject);
                debugger;
                var data = { Data: payload, UserContext: client.userContext };
 
                var ajaxRequest = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, true);
            
                ajaxRequest.done(function (data) {
 
             jsonData = data.Data;
                console.log(jsonData);
               $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(jsonData);
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper=$('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];

                });
            
    }

// Source: McLane Company, Inc (MCLANECO)_McLaneClientBussinessRules_1827.cs
// SetShipperAddressAsReturnAddress(element) // returns undefined
function SetShipperAddressAsReturnAddress(element)
    {
        debugger;
        
        var selectedShipper = "";
        
        if (typeof(element)==="object")
        {
            selectedShipper = $(element).find(":selected").text();
        }
        else if (typeof(element)==="string")
        {
            selectedShipper = element;
        }
        
        var cleanShipper = selectedShipper.replace("string:", "").replace("_", " ");
        
        if (cleanShipper != "" && cleanShipper != undefined )
        {
            
            if(cleanShipper =='16A4Y8 McLane')
            {
                $("#ddlShippingCharge").val("CustomerOrVendor");
            }
            else
            {
             $("#ddlShippingCharge").val("");   
            }
            
            SetShippingCharges(cleanShipper);
            
            var userMethodParams = { "action": "SetShipperAddressAsReturnAddress", "SelectedShipper": cleanShipper};
            
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
            
            var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
            
            if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
                client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
            } 
            else {
                    var json = DecodeReturnString(response.Data);
                    $('[name="company"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Company);
                    $('[name="contact"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Contact);
                    $('[name="address1"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Address1);
                    $('[name="address2"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Address2);
                    $('[name="address3"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Address3);
                    $('[name="city"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.City);
                    $('[name="stateProvince"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.StateProvince);
                    $('[name="postalCode"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.PostalCode);
                    $('[name="country"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Country);
                    vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = json.Address;
                }
        }
        
    }

// Source: Memorial Sloan-Kettering Cancer Center  (MSKCC)_MSKCC_Reference_Rules_63.cs
// updateDryIceRegulationSet() // returns void
    function updateDryIceRegulationSet() {
        debugger;
        $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.hazmatdryIceBtn"]', 'click', function() {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $dryIceRegulationSet = $('[ng-model="vm.dryIceInfo.DryIceRegulationSet"]');
                if ($dryIceRegulationSet.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $dryIceRegulationSet.find('option[label="Regulations Not Specified"]').remove();
                }
            }, 50);
        });
    }

// Source: Meta Platforms (API Shipping) (METAPLATFORMSAPISHIPPING)_Meta Thin Client Profile CBR_1868.cs
// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        vm = this.vm;
        if (location == '/') {
            document.location = '#!/shipping';
        }

        if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function() {
                if (window.jQuery) {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    $('button[ng-click="vm.showPendingShipmentModal()"]').click();
                }
            }, 50);

            var evaluateServices = setInterval(function() {
                $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)', 'change', function(e) {
                    console.log("Listening!");
                    clearInterval(evaluateServices);
                });
            }, 50);
        }
    };

// this.PostRate(shipmentRequest, rateResults) // returns void
this.PostRate = function(shipmentRequest, rateResults) 
    {   
        const dateToday = new Date();

        var selectedDeliverDate = this.vm.deliverDate;

        LogRateInformationToConsole(shipmentRequest, rateResults);
        if (!shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) 
        {
            ApplyRulesWithoutServiceRequested(shipmentRequest,rateResults,dateToday);
        }
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) 
        {
            ApplyRulesWithServiceRequested(shipmentRequest,rateResults,dateToday);
        }
        if (rateResults)        
        {
            var ratedServiceArrivalDateString = GetArriveDate(rateResults[0].PackageDefaults.ArriveDate);
            var ratedServiceArrivalAsDate = stringToDate(ratedServiceArrivalDateString, dateFormat, "-");    
            var expectedDeliveryDate = stringToDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5, dateFormat, "-");
            if (expectedDeliveryDate <= ratedServiceArrivalAsDate)
            {
                $('input[ng-model="vm.deliverDate.value"]').val(formatDate(ratedServiceArrivalAsDate)).change();   
            }
        }
    };

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) 
    {            
        //Services configured in Pending Shipments Profile Field Options
        var backup2DADomesticService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17; //UPSAPI.UPS.2DA        
        var backupNDADomesticService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference18; //UPSAPI.UPS.NDA        
        var backupExpeditedIntlService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference19; //UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED        
        var backupExpressIntlService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20; //UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS        

        $('body').on('click', 'table[aria-describedby="Pending Shipments"] input[type="button"]', this.vm, 
        function(e) 
        {
            $('input[ng-model="vm.deliverDate.value"]').val(e.data.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference5).change();
            if (e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service) 
            {
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference8"]').val(e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').val(backup2DADomesticService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference18"]').val(backupNDADomesticService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19"]').val(backupExpeditedIntlService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').val(backupExpressIntlService).change();
            }
        });
    };

// function ApplyRulesWithoutServiceRequested(shipmentRequest, rateResults, dateToday) // returns void
function ApplyRulesWithoutServiceRequested(shipmentRequest,rateResults,dateToday)
    {            
        if (stringToDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5, dateFormat, "-") <= dateToday) 
            {
                $('input[ng-model="vm.deliverDate.value"]').val(formatDate(getTomorrowDate())).change();

                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val(formatDate(getTomorrowDate())).change();
            } 
            else if (rateResults) 
            {                
                var fullArriveDate = GetArriveDate(rateResults[0].PackageDefaults.ArriveDate);

                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val(fullArriveDate).change();
            }   
    }

// function UpdateFields(dateValue, applyBackupService) // returns void
function UpdateFields(dateValue,applyBackupService)
    {
        $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val(dateValue).change();
        
        if(applyBackupService)
        {
            $('input[ng-model="vm.deliverDate.value"]').val(formatDate(getTomorrowDate())).change();
        }
        
    }

// function BackupServiceRequired(rateResults, shipmentRequest) // returns boolean
function BackupServiceRequired(rateResults,shipmentRequest)
    {
        var ratedArriveDate = GetStringArriveDate(rateResults[0].PackageDefaults.ArriveDate);

        var formattedArriveDate = stringToDate(ratedArriveDate, dateFormat, "-");

        var requestedDeliveryDate = stringToDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5, dateFormat, "-");

        var applyBackupService = (requestedDeliveryDate < formattedArriveDate);

        return applyBackupService;
    }

// function ApplyRulesWithServiceRequested(shipmentRequest, rateResults, dateToday) // returns void
function ApplyRulesWithServiceRequested(shipmentRequest,rateResults,dateToday)
    {
        var requestedServiceSymbol = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol;
        var backupNDADomesticService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference18; //UPSAPI.UPS.NDA        
        var backupExpressIntlService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20; //UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS  
        var serviceToBeReturned = '';
        var domestic = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === "US";

        rateResults.slice()
                   .forEach(function(item, index, object) 
        {            
            if (!requestedServiceSymbol) 
            {
                requestedServiceSymbol = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol;
            }

            serviceToBeReturned = requestedServiceSymbol;

            var requestedServiceIsFoundAsRateResult = (item.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);

            if (requestedServiceIsFoundAsRateResult) 
            {                                           
                console.log("Found requested service in position: " + index + "of rate results");

                var applyBackupService = BackupServiceRequired(rateResults,shipmentRequest);

                if (applyBackupService)
                {
                    if (domestic) 
                    {
                        serviceToBeReturned = backupNDADomesticService;                

                        UpdateFields(formatDate(getTomorrowDate(),true));  
                    }                
                    else
                    {
                        serviceToBeReturned = backupExpressIntlService;

                        rateResults.forEach(function(item, index, object) 
                        {
                            if (item.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === backupExpressIntlService) 
                            {
                                UpdateFields(formatDate(GetArriveDate(item.PackageDefaults.ArriveDate)),applyBackupService);                  
                            }
                        });                       
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    if (rateResults) 
                    {
                        var fullArriveDate = GetArriveDate(rateResults[0].PackageDefaults.ArriveDate);

                        UpdateFields(fullArriveDate,false);                         
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

// function LogRateInformationToConsole(shipmentRequest, rateResults) // returns void
function LogRateInformationToConsole(shipmentRequest, rateResults) 
    {
        var ratedServices ='';      
        
        console.log ("Requested Delivery Date" + stringToDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5, dateFormat, "-"));

        for (let i = 0; i< rateResults.length;i++)
        {
            if (rateResults[i].PackageDefaults.Service && rateResults[i].PackageDefaults.ArriveDate)
            {
                ratedServices += "Rate Result Position: " + i + " Service:" + rateResults[i].PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol + " Arrive: " + GetStringArriveDate(rateResults[i].PackageDefaults.ArriveDate);
                ratedServices += "\n";
            }
            else
            {
                ratedServices += "Rate Result Position: " + i + " Service: "+ rateResults[i].PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol + " Arrive: NA";
                ratedServices += "\n";
            }
        }

        console.log(ratedServices);
    }

// Source: MGMResorts (MGMRESOR)_Inbound Client Rules_1648.cs
// sleep(milliseconds) // returns void
    function sleep(milliseconds) {
        const date = Date.now();
        let currentDate = null;
        do {
            currentDate = Date.now();
        } while (currentDate - date < milliseconds);
    }

// Source: MGMResorts (MGMRESOR)_Outbound Client Rules_1649.cs
// decodeReturnString(data) // returns data with HTML entities decoded, or undefined on error
    function decodeReturnString(data) {
        try {
            data.Data = $('<div />').html(data.Data).text();
            if (data.ErrorMessage) {
                data.ErrorMessage = $('<div />').html(data.ErrorMessage).text();
            }
            return data;
        }
        catch (error) {
            console.log(error);
            //console.log(data);
        }
    }

// function Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {

        //uncomment this to auto get weight
        this.vm.getWeight = customGetWeight;
        debugger;

        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }//end of this.shipping

// function PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {

        //enable this to get weight auto at order load time
        this.vm.getWeight();
		debugger;
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
        checkForCancelled(this.vm);
        sumCommodities();

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

        function checkForCancelled(view) {

            var $misc19 = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19"]');

            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if ($misc19.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);

                        if ($misc19.val() == "T") {
                            debugger;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip = true;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisablePendingShipment = true;
                            $("input[value=\"Ship (F12)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Rate (F9)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Save\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            alert("This order is marked as Cancelled. Please load a new order");
                        }
                    }
                }, 50);

            }
        }
		

        function sumCommodities()
        {
            var commoditiesValue = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents.map(m => +m.Quantity * +m.UnitValue.Amount);
            var commTotal = 0.00;
            if(!commoditiesValue || Array.isArray(commoditiesValue ) || arr.commoditiesValue  !== 0)
            {
                for (let i = 0; i < commoditiesValue.length; i++) {
                    commTotal += commoditiesValue[i];
                  }
            }
            $('#SumCommTotal').text('Commodity Total: $' + commTotal);
        }
    }

    }

// Source: NAGINA INTERNATIONAL (NAGINA)_ISMEA_FTP_1585.cs
// getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// getUserContext() // returns void
function getUserContext() {
        debugger;
        if (userContext === undefined) {
            $.get({ url: "api/usercontext/GET", async:false })
            .done(function (data) {
               userContext = data;
            })
        }
    }

// Source: National Collectors Mint (NACOMI)_NCM Trial CBR_2467.cs
// loadWeight() // returns void
        function loadWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration === undefined) return;
            var scale = this.profile.ScaleConfiguration;
            var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read';
            var data = {
                'PortType': scale.ScaleDefinition.PortType,
                'Port': scale.Port,
                'UsbVid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbVid,
                'UsbPid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbPid,
                'RequestCommand': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestCommand,
                'BaudRate': scale.ScaleDefinition.BaudRate,
                'StopBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.StopBits,
                'Parity': scale.ScaleDefinition.Parity,
                'DataBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.DataBits,
                'RequestTimeout': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestTimeout,
                'HostAddress': scale.HostAddress,
                'RegexPattern': scale.ScaleDefinition.RegexPattern,
                'DeviceParser': scale.ScaleDefinition.DeviceParserType,
                'DeviceName': scale.ScaleDefinition.Name,
                'Handshake': scale.ScaleDefinition.Handshake,
                'RetryCount': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryCount,
                'RetryDelay': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryDelay
            };
            var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: data, async: false }).responseJSON;
            if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                    "Amount": ret.Weight,
                    "Units": ret.WeightUnit === null ? "LB" : ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                };


            } else {
                client.alert.Danger(this.translations.Common.ErrorCode + " : " + ret.ErrorCode + "  " + ret.ErrorMessage);
            }            
        }

// this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, context, codeReference) // returns address book entries or undefined
    this.GetAddressBookEntries = function (addressBook, context, codeReference) {
        if (addressBook != undefined) {
            var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Code", FieldValue: codeReference, Operator: 0 }] };
            var data = { AddressBookIds: [addressBook.Id], SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
            var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false);
            if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
                client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
            } else {
                if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
                    client.alert.Danger('Address Book Entries: No address found in "' + addressBookName + '" address book');
                } else {
                    return response.AddressBookEntries;
                }
            }
        }
    }

// this.thinClientAPIRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns responseJSON
    this.thinClientAPIRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON
    }

// Info(msg) // returns void
                Info: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-success alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-info').show();
                }

// Success(msg) // returns void
                Success: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
                }

// Danger(msg) // returns void
                Danger: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-success');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
                }

// Source: Nexus (NEXUS)_Nexus CBR Aug 2022_1798.cs
// GetAddressBook(addressBookName, context) // returns the first matching address book object or undefined
    this.GetAddressBook = function (addressBookName, context) {
        var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Name", FieldValue: addressBookName, Operator: 0 }] };
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks', data, false);
        if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
            client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
        } else {
            if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
                client.alert.Danger('Address Book: "' + addressBookName + '" does not exist');                
            } else {
                return response.AddressBooks[0];
            }
        }
    }

// GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, context, codeReference) // returns matching address book entries or undefined
    this.GetAddressBookEntries = function (addressBook, context, codeReference) {
        if (addressBook != undefined) {
            var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Code", FieldValue: codeReference, Operator: 0 }] };
            var data = { AddressBookIds: [addressBook.Id], SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
            var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries', data, false);
            if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
                client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
            } else {
                if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
                    client.alert.Danger('Address Book Entries: No address found in "' + addressBookName + '" address book');
                } else {
                    return response.AddressBookEntries;
                }
            }
        }
    }

// thinClientAPIRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns the response JSON from the ShipExec service request
    this.thinClientAPIRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON
    }

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();

                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').show();//.hide();
                            
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Third Party Options")').show();//.hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').show();//.hide();

                            //International
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').show();//.hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Validate Address"]').show();//.hide();

                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.IsUpdateAddressBookEntry"]').show();//.hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').show();//.hide();

                            $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').show();
                            
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Who pays Duties and Taxes")').show();//.hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').show();//.hide();

                        }
                    }
                }
            }, 125);
        }
    };

    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (typeof shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress !== "undefined") shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Code = "";
        this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference14.IsRequired = false;
    };

    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = GetCustom('Custom10','User', shipmentRequest);
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = GetCustom('Custom10','User', shipmentRequest);

        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges == "consignee" || shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.DutiesAndTaxes == "receiver") {
            SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest);
        }

        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference18 === "PPO") {
                //PPO
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference16;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference17;
			}else
			{
                //Non PPO
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference14;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference15;
            }
        }
    }

    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        debugger;
        if (typeof shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 !== "undefined") 
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = "";
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

	function GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType, ShipmentRequest){
			var customData = null;
			var returnValue = "";
			if(customDataType === "User") customData = ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
			if(customDataType === "To") customData = ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeAddress.CustomData;
			
			if(customData) {
				customData.forEach(function (customField){
					if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
				})
			}
			return returnValue;
	};
}

// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        vm = this.vm;
        if (location == "/shipping") {
            // Select PPO vs Non-PPO
                    
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference18"]', 'change', function () {
                var $referenceOptions = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference18"]');
                if ($referenceOptions.val() === "PPO") {
                    //alert("PPO" + $referenceOptions.val());
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference14.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference15.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = true;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.IsRequired = true;
                    $('label:contains("Enter Name of Shipment Requestor")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference14"]').hide();
                    $('label:contains("NIKE Cost/Profit Center Bill To")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference15"]').hide();


                    $('label:contains("C/N CARTON ID NUMBER 1 Per Carton")').show();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference16"]').show();
                    $('label:contains("PO# (Begins with 35, 45)")').show();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').show();
                } else if ($referenceOptions.val() === "Non-PPO") {
                    //alert("Non-PPO" + $referenceOptions.val());
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference14.IsRequired = true;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference15.IsRequired = true;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.IsRequired = false;
                    $('label:contains("Enter Name of Shipment Requestor")').show();

                var $billOption = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.DutiesAndTaxes"]');
                //   alert($billOption.val());
                if ($billOption.val() == "thirdParty") {

                        consigneeFound = true;
                    }
                    var loaded = tpbFound && consigneeFound;


                    // console.log(`is consignee loaded: ${loaded}`)

                    if (loaded) {
                        debugger;
                        if ($thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').length > 0) {
                            startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();

            SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest);
        }

            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference18 === "PPO") {
                //PPO
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference16;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference17;

// SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns void
function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        debugger;
        if (typeof shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 !== "undefined") 
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = "";
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
	this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
	    vm = this.vm;
	    //console.log(vm);
		globalVar = location;
		if (globalVar === '/createbatch') {
			var checkExist = setInterval(function() {
				if (window.jQuery) {
					/* Stop the timer */
					clearInterval(checkExist);
					var emailText = "";
					var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
					Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag) {
						if (tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!", "").trim();
					});
					let i = emailText.indexOf("@");
					$('input[name="batchReference"]').val(emailText.substring(0, i) + GetDateTimeToString()).change();

				}
			}, 50);
			
			HighlightWrongOrderNumber();
		}
		
		
        if (globalVar === '/scanship') {
        	HighlightWrongOrderNumber();
        }
		
		if (globalVar === '/history' || globalVar === '/groupmanager' ) {
			var emailText = "";
			var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
			Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag) {
				if (tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!", "").trim();
			});
			let i = emailText.indexOf("@");
			if(emailText.substring(0, i)==='demo0')
			{ ReplaceAccountNumberWithXXXXXX();} 
        }
        
        if(globalVar === '/closemanifest'){
            // Provide a default label function to avoid "undefined" in the select
            vm.getManifestLabel = function(item) {
                // Show nothing or a placeholder until real data is loaded
                return item && item.Name ? item.Name : '';
            };
            getDates(vm);
        }
        
	}

// function ClientBusinessRules() // returns undefined
function ClientBusinessRules() {
    var vm;
    var pkgweight;
    var jsonParse;
    var scale = "EC";

    this.PageLoaded = function(location) { 
    if(location === "/")
     document.location = "#!/shipping";
     
    if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") 
    {
      var checkExist = setInterval(function() 
      {
          if (window.jQuery) 
          {
              /* Stop the timer. */
              clearInterval(checkExist);
              $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function(e) { $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide(); });
            }
          }, 50);
      }
    }

    this.Keystroke = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {

    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userInfo, userParams) {
        //shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;
        //validateConsigneeAddress(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee);
                
    }

    this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
    }

    this.PreProcessBatch = function(batchReference, actions, params, vm) {

    }

    this.PreVoid = function(pkg, userParams) {
    }

    this.PostVoid = function(pkg) {
    }

    this.PrePrint = function(document, localPort) {
    }

    this.PostPrint = function(document) {
