    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;        
        //$.get({ url: "http://localhost:9091/api/websites/96659", cache: false })
        //    .fail(function (e) {
        //        alert('The Scale Service may not be running. Please check to make sure the ShipExec Client Service is running');
        //    });
        //}
     
        if(scale == 'EC')   {
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: "http://localhost:9093/api/websites/96659",
                async: false,
                cache: false,
                success: function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    //alert(result);
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5= result;
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference7= "EC";                       
                },
                error: function(jqXhr, exception) {
                alert("Please check the Express Cube Scale Service to make sure the service is running " + exception);                    
                }
            });
        }
    }

    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount;                        

        if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 !== null)              {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 == 'YES' ) {
                shipmentRequest.AlertTitle = "ShipExec Alert";
                shipmentRequest.AlertMessage = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference + " has previously shipped today " + shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ShipDate +  ". Click Yes to ship again. Click No to abort.";
                angular.element('[ng-model="AlertModal"]').modal('show');
            }
        }
        
        if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 !== null)              {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 !== 'ADDRESS1MATCH' ) {
                //alert("The Address Line 1 was not matched. Please run Address Validation prior to shipping this package");
                this.vm.alerts = [{type:'danger', msg:'The Address Line 1 was not matched. Please run Address Validation prior to shipping this package'}];
            }   
        }
    }

    this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;        
        shipmentRequest.AlertTitle = '';
        shipmentRequest.AlertMessage = '';
        angular.element('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').focus();
        
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper="OEMCONNECT";
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms="SHIPPER";
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging="CUSTOM";
        //var Service = { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.GND", Name: "UPS Ground (CSAdapter)" };
        var Service = { Symbol: "OEMCONNE.Custom.SPPS", Name: "UPS SurePost lb or Greater" };        
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = Service;
        var ConsigneeAddress = {Country: "US"};
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = ConsigneeAddress;

// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;        
        //$.get({ url: "http://localhost:9091/api/websites/96659", cache: false })
        //    .fail(function (e) {
        //        alert('The Scale Service may not be running. Please check to make sure the ShipExec Client Service is running');
        //    });

        if(scale == 'EC')   {
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: "http://localhost:9093/api/websites/96659",
                async: false,
                cache: false,
                success: function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    //alert(result);
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5= result;
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference7= "EC";                       
                },
                error: function(jqXhr, exception) {
                alert("Please check the Express Cube Scale Service to make sure the service is running " + exception);                    
                }
            });
        }
    }

            });
        }	    
    }

this.PageLoaded = function(location){
        if(location =="/shipping"){
            // $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] input[name="PostalCode"]', 'keydown', function() {
            //    alert('hello');
            //});
            
            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="ThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'change', function() {
                var $thirdPartyBilling = $('name-address[address-property-name="ThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]');
                if($thirdPartyBilling.val() != "string:--------------------"){
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="ThirdPartyBillingAddress"] button[title="Search Addresses"]').click();
                    //alert($thirdPartyBilling.val());
                } 
            })
            
            var startTime = new Date();
            var pageLoaded = setInterval(function() {
                if ((new Date().getTime() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000 >= 2) {
                    clearInterval(pageLoaded);
                    console.log('clearinterval')
                } else {
                    var tpbFound = false;
                    var consigneeFound = false;
                    var $thirdPartyBillingAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="ThirdPartyBillingAddress"]');
                    var tpbSearchAddress = $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]');
                    var $consignee = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                    var consineeSearchAddress = $consignee.find('[title="Search Addresses"]');
                    if ($thirdPartyBillingAddress.length && tpbSearchAddress.length) {
                        tpbFound = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($consignee.length && consineeSearchAddress.length) {
                        consigneeFound = true;
                    }
                    var loaded = tpbFound && consigneeFound;
                    

                    console.log(`is consignee loaded: ${loaded}`)

                    if (loaded) {
                        if($thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').length > 0){
                            startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);
                            
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Validate Address"]').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.IsUpdateAddressBookEntry"]').hide();
                        }   $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();
                        
                    }
                }
            }, 125);


        }
    }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams){
        console.log(shipmentRequest);
                console.log(userParams);
        
        jobAndWBSInPrintLabel(shipmentRequest);

            var selection = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Code;
            if(selection && selection !== "---------------------"){
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
            }else{
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = false;
            }
        }
        if(typeof shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod != "undefined")shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnDelivery = true;
        
    }

// Source: Philip Morris USA Domestic (PMUSADomestic)_PMUSADom_Reference_Rules_56.cs
// GetEmail() // returns the extracted email text string
   GetEmail(){
      var emailText = "";
      var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a"); 
      Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag){
         if(tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!","").trim(); 
      });
      return emailText;
   }

// Source: PRA Developer (PRADeveloper)_PRA Intl Business Rules_1523.cs
// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
       
        /* Only apply these functions to the shipping page. */
        if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") {
            $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
                $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
            })

            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if ((window.jQuery !== undefined) && ($('select[name=Country]').length > 0)) {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);

                    /* Register the event that fires when a user clicks the 'Reset' button on the main page. */
                    $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.newShipment()"]:eq(0)', 'click', function (e) {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                    });

                    /* Disable the ThirdPartyBilling edit button. */
                    $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);

                    /* For select boxes which are enabled, remove the default country of United States. */
                    $('select[name=Country][disabled!=disabled]').prop('selectedIndex', 0);

                    /* Trying to fix a bug where the Ship From country select element is disabled and set to the wrong country. */
                    /* Enable the element. */
                    $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').prop('disabled', false);

                    /* Hide the End Of Day dropdown menu. */
                    $('ul.nav.navbar-nav li.dropdown:eq(1) > a.dropdown-toggle').hide();

                    /* Change captions for tabs when processing return shipments. */
                    /* Register the event on change. */
                    $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]', 'change', function (e) {
                        var isReturn = $(this).val().length > 0;
                        ReturnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
                        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery = isReturn;
                    });

                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                } /* if ((window.jQuery... */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */

        } /* if (window.location.hash... */
    };

// this.PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) // returns undefined
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) {
        debugger;
        if (addressName !== '' && addressName !== 'ThirdPartyBillingAddress') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if (($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().length > 0) && ($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().length > 0)) {

                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    /* The values are stored in the format of 'string:CC'.  We only want the CC. */
                    var shipToCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().replace('string:', '');
                    var shipFromCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().replace('string:', '');

                    /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
                    if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
                        /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
                        SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                    }
                    else {
                        /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
                        if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                            SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                        }

                        //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
                    }
                } /* if ($('div.modal-dialog.modal-md:visible') */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */
        }
    };

// this.EmailNotificationAddress(event) // returns undefined
    this.EmailNotificationAddress = function (event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];
        debugger;
        // if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
        //     SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
        //     SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // } else {
        //     SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // }

        if (ngModelName == 'ShipNotificationEmail') {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName == 'DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail') {
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName == 'DeliveryNotificationEmail') {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    };

// HideRenameCommodityContents() // returns void
function HideRenameCommodityContents() {
        debugger;
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var formCommo = $('form[name="commoditiesModalForm"]');
            if (formCommo.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                var divOD = $('div[property="CommodityContent.OriginDescription"]');
                divOD.hide();
                var divCC = $('div[property="CommodityContent.CommodityCondition"]');
                divCC.hide();

                //Tabs
                var ulNavs = formCommo.find('ul[class="nav nav-tabs"]');
                var commTabs = ulNavs.eq(0);
                var liTabs = commTabs.find('li');
                for(var i=0; i<=liTabs.length; i++) {
                    if (i !== 0 && i !== 4 && i !== 5)
                    {
                        var element = liTabs.eq(i);
                        element.hide();
                    }
                }
                
                //Restricted Article
                var divs = formCommo.find('div[ng-repeat="raTypes in vm.profile.RestrictedArticleTypes"]');
                var numOfElements = divs.length;
                for(var i=0; i<=numOfElements; i++) {
                    if (i < 7)
                    {
                        var element = divs.eq(i);
                        element.hide();
                    }
                }
                
                //Renaming NAFTA to CUSMA
                var liNAFTA = $('li[index="4"]');
                liNAFTA.hide();
                var ahrefNAFTA = liNAFTA.find('a[ng-click="select($event)"]');
                RenameElement(ahrefNAFTA, 'CUSMA', 'CUSMA');
                var divNAFTA = $('div[property="CommodityContent.NaftaProducer"]');
                var lblNAFTAProducer = divNAFTA.find('label');
                RenameElement(lblNAFTAProducer, 'CUSMA Producer Indicator', 'Indicateur ACEUM pour les producteurs');

                //RemovingCurrencyCommodity();

            }
        }, 50);
        
    }

// ReplaceHazmatHeader() // returns void
function ReplaceHazmatHeader(){
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var divHaz = $('div[class="modal-dialog modal-lg"]');
            if (divHaz.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                var div1 = divHaz.find('div[class="modal-content"]');
                var div2 = div1.find('div[class="modal-content ng-scope"]');
                var div3 = div2.find('div[class="modal-header"]');
                var h4 = div3.find('h4');
                //debugger;
                if (h4.text() == 'Add Hazmat Content')
                {
                    RenameElement(h4, 'Add Dangerous Goods Content', 'Ajouter du contenu sur les marchandises dangereuses');
                }
                var form = $('form[name="hazmatModalForm"]');
                div1 = form.find('div[class="modal-body"]');

                var div3 = div2.find('div[ng-show="vm.hazmatContentDiv == \'labelcategory\'"]');
                var div4 = div3.find('div[class="row col-md-12"]');
                var div5 = div4.find('div[class="col-md-6 ng-isolate-scope"]');
                var div = div5.find('div[class="form-group"]');
                var lbl = div.find('label');
                //debugger;
                RenameElement(lbl.eq(0), 'Dangerous Goods Labels', 'Étiquettes de marchandises dangereuses')

                var na = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.hazmatContent.HazmatInfectiousResponsibleParty"]');
                var divRow = na.find('div[class="row"]');
                var div1 = divRow.find('div[class="col-md-3 small text-left no-bottom-left no-bottom-right"]');
                div1.hide();

                //Removing Hazmat UOM
                $('select[ng-model="vm.hazmatContent.HazmatQuantity.Units"]> option[value="string:FOZ"]').remove();
                $('select[ng-model="vm.hazmatContent.HazmatQuantity.Units"]> option[value="string:GAL"]').remove();
                $('select[ng-model="vm.hazmatContent.HazmatQuantity.Units"]> option[value="string:GLB"]').remove();
                $('select[ng-model="vm.hazmatContent.HazmatQuantity.Units"]> option[value="string:OZ"]').remove();
                $('select[ng-model="vm.hazmatContent.HazmatQuantity.Units"]> option[value="string:PT"]').remove();
                $('select[ng-model="vm.hazmatContent.HazmatQuantity.Units"]> option[value="string:LB"]').remove();
                $('select[ng-model="vm.hazmatContent.HazmatQuantity.Units"]> option[value="string:QT"]').remove();

// HideGroupManager() // returns void
function HideGroupManager(){
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var select = $('select[ng-change="vm.groupTypeChange()"]');
            if (select.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                //debugger;
                select.children('option[value="GUARDIAN"]').remove();
                select.children('option[value="TRADE_DIRECT"]').remove();
                $('body').delegate('select[ng-change="vm.groupTypeChange()"]', 'change', RenameShipperGroupManager); 
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// function customUserMethod() // returns undefined
function customUserMethod () {
        debugger;
        var dateSelected = $('#exportDate').val();
        var shipper = $('#gateway :selected').text();
        var carrier = $('#carrier :selected').text();
        
        if (carrier === 'UPS')
        {
            carrier = 'CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS';
        }
        else
        {
            carrier = 'CONNECTSHIP_DHLXMLPI.DHL';
        }

        var data = { DateSelected: dateSelected, Shipper: shipper, Carrier: carrier};
        var payload = { UserContext: client.userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) };
        var result = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', payload, false).responseJSON;
        
        debugger;
        if (result.ErrorCode > 0 || result == undefined) {
            client.alert.Danger(result.ErrorCode + ': ' + result.ErrorMessage);
        } else if (result.Message != undefined || result.Message != "") {
            client.alert.Success(result.Message);
        } else {
            client.alert.Success(result.Message);
        }
    }

// function CopyShipperList() // returns undefined
function CopyShipperList() {
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
        debugger;
        let shipper = $('shipper-carrier');
            if (shipper.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                let div1 = shipper.find('div');
                let div2 = div1.find('div');
                let div3 = div2.find('div');
                let dpShip = div3.find('Select[ng-model="vm.selectedShipper"]');
                let dpOpt = dpShip.find('option');
                var $options = dpOpt.clone();
                $('#gateway').append($options);
            }
        }, 50);
        
        
    }

// Source: R.BCC EXPORTERS PRIVATE LIMITED (R.BCC)_ISMEA_FTP_1716.cs
// getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// getUserContext() // returns void
function getUserContext() {
        debugger;
        if (userContext === undefined) {
            $.get({ url: "api/usercontext/GET", async:false })
            .done(function (data) {
               userContext = data;
            })
        }
    }

// function PreLoad(value, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
		//debugger;
		//getWeight(this.vm);   // TODO: disabled until scale issue resolved
		
		// signed checkbox value
		let signedChecked = $('.form-check[property=MiscReference19]').find('input').prop('checked');
		if (signedChecked === true) {
			userParams.autoship = "autoship";
		}
	};

// function PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === undefined) {
			alert("No service selected!");
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null  && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage === 'validate')
		{
			// click validate button
			$('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find('button[ng-click="validate(nameaddress)"]').click();
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(0, 4) === 'pop:') {
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== '')
		{
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage);
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}
		
		//getWeight(this.vm);   // TODO: disabled until scale issue resolved
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship')
		{
			if (!this.vm.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip) {
				this.vm.checkShip();
			}
		}
	};

// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
		//debugger;

		if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight !== undefined) {
			userParams.weight = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Amount;
		}
	};

// function PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns undefined
    this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== 0)
		{
			alert("Shipping error: " + shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode);
		}
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = false;    // signature_required_checkbox
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = true;    // autoship_checkbox
	};

// function downloadFromCin7API() // returns undefined
    this.downloadFromCin7API = function() {
		//debugger;
		let data = { Action: 'Download_Orders', Params: ''};
		
		downloadOrders = true;
		toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);

		// call SBR UserMethod to access Cin7 API to download orders
		$.post({
			url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
			headers: clientService.authorizationToken(),
			data: {
			    UserContext: client.userContext,
			    Data: JSON.stringify(data)
			}
		}).done(function (data) {
		    //debugger;
			downloadOrders = false;
		    toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);
		    
			if (data.Data === true) {
				alert('Download successful!');
			}
			else {
				alert('Download was not successful');
			}
		}).fail(function (err) {
		    //debugger;
			downloadOrders = false;
		    toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);
			console.log(err.responseJSON);
			alert('Download was not successful');
		});
	}

// Source: Rite Kem (RITEKEM)_RiteKem_1637.cs
// getHazmatReport() // returns the $.post request object or undefined
function getHazmatReport() {
        debugger;
        var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
        var context = client.userContext;
        var shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedShipper"] option:selected').val();
        if (shipper) {
            var searchCriteria = { DateStart: $('input[ng-model="vm.dtstart"]').val(), DateEnd: $('input[ng-model="vm.dtend"]').val(), Shipper: shipper };
            var data = { Action: "HazmatReport", Content: JSON.stringify(searchCriteria) };
           return $.post({ url:shipExecServiceUrl +'/UserMethod',
                  data: {UserContext: client.userContext, Data:JSON.stringify(data)}, headers: authorizationToken},
                function (response, status, xhr) {
                    downloadFile(shipper, response["Data"]);
                }
            ).done(function () {
            });
        }
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {    
        this.vm.hideSaveAddress = true;
        this.vm.isUpdateAddressBookEntry = true;
        this.vm.hideAddressSearch = true;
        this.vm.thirdPartyBillingDisabled = thirdPartyBillingDisabled;
        debugger;
        
        client.shipping.consignee.searchAddresses.addButtonLabel(' ' + this.vm.translations.Common.SearchAddresses);
        client.shipping.consignee.validateAddress.addButtonLabel(' ' + this.vm.translations.Common.ValidateAddress);

        function thirdPartyBillingDisabled(isDisabled) {
            var $tpb = $('div[property="ThirdPartyBilling"]');
            if (isDisabled) {
                this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = false;
                this.thirdPartyBilling();
                $tpb.find('input').attr('disabled', true);
                $tpb.find('label').addClass('disabled');
            } else {
                $tpb.find('input').removeAttr('disabled');
                $tpb.find('label').removeClass('disabled');
            }
        }
    }

    }

// Source: SAVERS (SAVERS)_Savers Client Side Rules_1715.cs
// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest)
    {
    this.vm.shipMode = 0;
    this.vm.disableShipMode = true;
    filterPickupPaymentType();

        function filterPickupPaymentType() {
            var list = ['Pay by shipper account'];            
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var currencies = $('[ng-model="vm.pickup.PaymentType"] option');
                if (currencies.length) {
                    debugger;
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function (){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
        }
}

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns undefined
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {

    //debugger;

    //Map Store Number to ShipperReference
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = nameaddress.Code;

    //Set Default Services Based on From and To Countries		
    var fromCountry = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country;
    var toCountry = nameaddress.Country;

    //Email Address Mappings
	if(nameaddress.Email != null)
	{
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
	}

    //Store Address Book ID value in MiscReference20 to signify that consignee address came from Address Book and was not manually entered.
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = nameaddress.AddressBookId.toString();


    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.GND")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}
}

// Source: Sazerac (Sazerac)_Sazerac CBR_1680.cs
// ClientBusinessRules() // returns constructor-like object initializer
function ClientBusinessRules() {
    var vmTemp;

    var clientService = {
        config: $.getJSON({url:'config.json', async: false}).responseJSON,
        authorizationToken: function () {
            if (JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken"))) {
                return { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token };
            }
        }
    }

    var client = {
        userContext: function () {
            var userContextUrl = 'api/usercontext/GET';
            var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            if (shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http')) {
                var url = new URL(shipExecServiceUrl);
                userContextUrl = url.origin + '/' + userContextUrl;
            }
            var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
            return $.get({url: userContextUrl, headers: authorizationToken, async: false}).responseJSON;
        }()
    }

    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
    }

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        vmTemp = this.vm;
        
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            if ($('form[name="generalForm"]').length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                
                if ($('#ship_goods_type').length === 0) {
                    CreateCustomShippingElements(vmTemp);
                }
                // reset custom controls
                resetShipExec();

                //DJM 5/29/2020 Changes / Default Values for Frankfort Returns Shipper **************************
                var shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().replace('string:','');
                
                if (shipper == "FRANKFORT_RETURNS") {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery = true;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = "02-0200-61309";		
                }
            }
            
        }, 100);
       
    };

    function CreateCustomShippingElements(vm) {
        //debugger;
        //#region Create Ship Goods Type DropDown
        var shipGoodsType = "<div class='form-group col-md-12 no-left-right-padding'>" +
        "<div class='col-md-6 no-left-padding'>" +
        "<label for='search_input' style='margin-top: 6px'>What are you shipping? </label>" +
        "<select id='ship_goods_type' class='form-control'>" +
        "<option value='default' selected='selected'>Shipment Goods Type</option>" +
        "<option value='non_distilled'>Non Distilled Spirit</option>" +
        "<option value='non_sample'>Non Sample Case Goods</option>" +
        "<option value='sample'>Sample</option>" +
        "</select>" +
        "</div>" +
        "<div class='col-md-6'>" +
        "<div style='margin-top: 6px'>&nbsp;</div>" +
        "<label style='margin-right: 8%'><input id='third_party_rule' type='checkbox' ng-model='vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference19'>&nbsp; Third Party Rule</label>" +
        "<label><input id='adult_signature_required_rule' type='checkbox' ng-model='vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference20'>&nbsp; Adult Signature Required Rule</label>" +
        "</div>" +
        "</div>" +
        // Cost Code dropdown
        "<div class='col-md-6 no-left-padding'>" +
        "<label for='search_input' style='margin-top: 6px'>Person you are shipping for: </label>" +
        "<div class='col-md-12 no-left-right-padding'>" +
        "<div class='col-md-10 no-left-padding'><input id='search_input' type='text' name='inputsearch' class='form-control'></div>" +
        "<input id='searchButton' type='button' value='Search' class='btn btn-primary col-md-2'>" +
        "</div></div>" +
        "<div class='col-md-6 no-right-padding'>" +
        "<div style='margin-top: 6px'>&nbsp;</div>" +
        "<select id='costcodes' class='form-control'>" +
        "<option value='Default' selected='selected'>Select Cost Center</option></select>" +
        "</div>";
        
        $('form[name="generalForm"]').find('textarea').after(shipGoodsType);
        $('#costcodes').hide();

        //#endregion

        //#region Create Ship Goods List Select Event
        $("#ship_goods_type").change(function () {
            //Capture ship goods type and store
            var shipGoodsType = $('#ship_goods_type').val();
            vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipGoodsType;

            //Assign shipper in listbox
            //$('#ctl00_cphContent_shipper_list').val('S_FREDERICKSBURG_VA');
        });
        //#endregion

        $('#third_party_rule').prop('checked', vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference19);
        $('#third_party_rule').change(function () {
            var thirdParty = $('#third_party_rule').prop('checked');
            vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = thirdParty;
        });

        $('#adult_signature_required_rule').prop('checked', vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference20);
        $('#adult_signature_required_rule').change(function () {
            var signatureRequired = $('#adult_signature_required_rule').prop('checked');
            vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = signatureRequired;
        });
        //#endregion

        //#region Click Search Button
        $("#searchButton").click(function() {
            //Remove drop-down control if it exists before creating a new one
            //$("#costcodes").remove();

            // added prefix to beginning of search value for UserMethod call, since method is used for other functions
            var searchName = "search|" + $('#search_input').val();

            if (searchName.length !== 0 && searchName != 'search|')
            {
                // reset dropdown
                $('#costcodes').off('change');
                $('#costcodes option:not(:first)').remove();
                $('#costcodes').hide();

                // call user method
                var params = searchName;

                //$.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
                //{
                //    UserContext: userContext,
                //    Data: JSON.stringify(params)
                
                // updated for 2.3
                $.post({
                    url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
                    data: {
                        UserContext: client.userContext,
                        Data: JSON.stringify(params)
                    },
                    headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
                }).done(function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    result = decodeReturnString(result);
                    if (result !== null && result !== undefined && result !== '') {
                        if (result.ErrorCode === 0 && result.Data !== undefined && !(typeof(result.Data) == 'string' && result.Data.indexOf('[Error]') == -1)) {
                            ParseJson(result.Data);
                        }
                        else {
                            //Display Error
                            alert(result.Data);
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        alert("No data was returned from search");
                    }
                }).fail(function (e) {
                    alert(e.message);
                });
            }
            else
            {
                alert("Please enter name of whom you are shipping for before clicking the search button.");
                $('#search_input').css('background-color', '#fffef0');
                $('#search_input').focus();
            }
        });
        //#endregion

        //#region Create Cost Code File Button
        var costCodeFileButton = "<span>" +
            "<input type='file' id='fileLoader' name='files' title='Load Cost Code File' style='display:none;'> " +
            "<button id='btnOpenFileDialog' value='Import New GL Code File' class='btn btn-xs btn-primary'>Import New GL Code File</button>" +
            "</span>";

        // add button beside Pending Shipments
        $("div.row.top-tool-bar").find("div.pull-left").append(costCodeFileButton);
        $("#fileLoader").change(function() {
            openFileDialog();
        });
        $("#btnOpenFileDialog").click(function() {
            $("#fileLoader").click();
        });
        //#endregion
    }

    //#region Open File Dialog
    /**
    * Get file name and convert to Bas64 Url
    * then call usermethod to send the data server side
    */
    function openFileDialog() {
        //debugger;
        var filesSelected = document.getElementById("fileLoader");

        if (filesSelected !== undefined) {
            const fileReader = new FileReader();

            if (filesSelected.files[0]) {
                fileReader.readAsDataURL(filesSelected.files[0]);
            }

            fileReader.onload = function (event) {
                var files = event.target.result;

                // Get base64 file data
                var contents = event.target.result.split(',')[1];

                // adding prefix to beginning of file data to send to user method
                var fileData = "file|" + contents;

                // $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
                // {
                //     UserContext: userContext,
                //     Data: JSON.stringify(fileData)

                // updated for 2.3
                $.post({
                    url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
                    data: {
                        UserContext: client.userContext,
                        Data: JSON.stringify(fileData)
                    },
                    headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
                }).done(function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    // result.Data should be unencoded [Success] or [Error] string
                    if (result.ErrorCode === 0 && result.Data !== undefined && result.Data.indexOf('[Error]') == -1) {
                        alert(result.Data);
                    }
                    else {
                        // display error
                        alert(result.Data);
                    }
                }).fail(function (e) {
                    alert(e.message);
                });
            };
        }
    }
    //#endregion

    // decode returned UserMethod data - SW 1/18/2022
    function decodeReturnString(data) {
        try {
            data.Data = JSON.parse($('<div />').html(data.Data).text());
            if (data.ErrorMessage) {
                data.ErrorMessage = $('<div />').html(data.ErrorMessage).text();
            }
            return data;
        }
        catch (error) {
            console.log(error);
            //console.log(data);
        }
    }

    //#region ParseJson
    function ParseJson(result) {
        //debugger;
        var jsonLoad = result; //jQuery.parseJSON(result);
       
        if (jsonLoad !== null && jsonLoad !== undefined)
        {
            $('#search_input').css('background-color', '#fffef0');
    
            //#region Build Drop-Down List
            var html = "";

            for (let i in jsonLoad.listData)
            {
                html += "<option value='" + jsonLoad.listData[i].glCode + "'>" + jsonLoad.listData[i].fullName + " " + jsonLoad.listData[i].glCode + "</option>";
            }
    
            if (jsonLoad.listData.length === 0)
            {
                alert("No records were returned from search")
            }
            else //More than one record returned
            {
                //$("#costcodes").remove();
                //$(html).insertAfter("#searchButton");
                $("#costcodes").append(html);
                $('#costcodes').change(function() {
                    populateShipExec();
                });
                $("#costcodes").show();
            }
    
        }
        else
        {
            alert("Error populating dropdown box --- " + jsonLoad.ErrorMessage);
        }
    
    }
    //#endregion
    
    //#region populateShipExec
    function populateShipExec() {
        //Get cost code value from selected value in drop down list
        var costcode = document.getElementById('costcodes').value;
        var fullitemtext = document.getElementById('costcodes').options[document.getElementById('costcodes').selectedIndex].text;
    
        //Populate Cost Code in shipper_reference field
        vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].ShipperReference = costcode;
    
        //Populate Full Value in Reference Field 3
        vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference3 = fullitemtext;
    
        //Reset ShipExec Controls
        //document.getElementById('costcodes').outerHTML = "";
        $('#costcodes').off('change');
        $('#costcodes option:not(:first)').remove();
        $('#costcodes').hide();
        ////resetShipExec();
        $('#search_input').val('');
        $('#search_input').css('background-color', '#fffef0');
    }
    //#endregion
    
    //#region Reset Custom Controls in ShipExec
    function resetShipExec() {    
        $('#search_input').val('');
        $('#search_input').css('background-color', '#fffef0');
        $('#ship_goods_type').val("default");
    }
    //#endregion
    
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        //var costCodeList = document.getElementById("costcodes");
        var costCodeList = $("#costcodes")[0];

        for (var i = 0; i < costCodeList.options.length; i++) {
            if (costCodeList.options[i].selected == true) {
                alert("SELECTED = " + costCodeList.options[i].innerText);

                // selected item        
                alert(costCodeList.options[i].loadValue);
            }
        }
    };

    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //debugger;
        var shipperSymbol = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper;

        //Skip Ship Goods Type Selection for these international shipper origins
        if (shipperSymbol != "SEGONZAC_FR" && shipperSymbol != "SURREY_UK" && shipperSymbol != "DUBLIN_IE" && shipperSymbol != "NAYANDA_IN" && shipperSymbol != "FRANKFORT_RETURNS") {
            var shipGoodsType = document.getElementById('ship_goods_type').options[document.getElementById('ship_goods_type').selectedIndex].value;
            var pkg1MiscRef4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
            //if (shipGoodsType == null || shipGoodsType == 'undefined' || shipGoodsType == '' || shipGoodsType == 'default')
            if (pkg1MiscRef4 == null || pkg1MiscRef4 == undefined || pkg1MiscRef4 == '' || shipGoodsType == 'default') {
                $("#ship_goods_type").val('default');
                //$('#ship_goods_type').css('background-color', '#FF3333');
                $('#ship_goods_type').focus();
                var errorMessage = "Error, You must select a Shipment Goods Type on the first package of the shipment";
                alert(errorMessage);
                return;
            }
        }

        //#region Require Field Validation
        if (shipperSymbol != "FRANKFORT_RETURNS") {
            //debugger;
            //var costCodeValue = $("#ctl00_cphContent_right_tabs_ref_tab_ref_ctrl_misc_ref_pane_content_misc_reference_3_txt").val();
            var costCodeValue = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
            if (costCodeValue == null || costCodeValue == undefined || costCodeValue == '') {
                $('#costcodes').focus();
                var errorMessage = "Error, You must select a Cost Code value on the first package of the shipment";
                alert(errorMessage);
            }
        }
        //#endregion

        var thirdParty = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference19;
        var adultSignature = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference20;

        userParams.third_party_rule = thirdParty;
        userParams.adult_signature_required_rule = adultSignature;
    };

    this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
        //#region Package Details
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].description;
        //#endregion

        //#region Reference
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference5 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5;
        //#endregion

        //#region User Data
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].UserData1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData1;
        //#endregion

        //#region Email Notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipNotificationEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationEmail;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationEmail;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;
        //#endregion

        //#region Get Scale Weight
        //get_weight_scale_btn_OnClick();
        if (vmTemp && vmTemp.profile.ScaleConfiguration !== undefined) {	// get Weight if button isn't disabled
			vmTemp.getWeight();
		}
        //#endregion
    };

}

// openFileDialog() // returns void
    function openFileDialog() {
        //debugger;
        var filesSelected = document.getElementById("fileLoader");

        if (filesSelected !== undefined) {
            const fileReader = new FileReader();

            if (filesSelected.files[0]) {
                fileReader.readAsDataURL(filesSelected.files[0]);
            }

            fileReader.onload = function (event) {
                var files = event.target.result;

                // Get base64 file data
                var contents = event.target.result.split(',')[1];

                // adding prefix to beginning of file data to send to user method
                var fileData = "file|" + contents;

                // $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
                // {
                //     UserContext: userContext,
                //     Data: JSON.stringify(fileData)

                // updated for 2.3
                $.post({
                    url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
                    data: {
                        UserContext: client.userContext,
                        Data: JSON.stringify(fileData)
                    },
                    headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
                }).done(function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    // result.Data should be unencoded [Success] or [Error] string
                    if (result.ErrorCode === 0 && result.Data !== undefined && result.Data.indexOf('[Error]') == -1) {
                        alert(result.Data);
                    }
                    else {
                        // display error
                        alert(result.Data);
                    }
                }).fail(function (e) {
                    alert(e.message);
                });
            };
        }
    }

                html += "<option value='" + jsonLoad.listData[i].glCode + "'>" + jsonLoad.listData[i].fullName + " " + jsonLoad.listData[i].glCode + "</option>";

        }
    
    }

// thinClientAPIRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns the jQuery AJAX POST request
    var thinClientAPIRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = client.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = client.getAuthorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken });
    }

// TestUserMethod() // returns Promise<void>
  TestUserMethod = async () =>
  {
    let that = this;
    window.localStorage.removeItem('cbrValues');

    const user = new User(this.userInformation);
    const _ = await user.GetUserMethodObjects().then((data) =>
    {
      let m = {};
      m.MethodName = 'GetTestData';
      m.MethodData = 0;

      let ajaxObject = {};
      ajaxObject.UserContext = user.UserContext;
      ajaxObject.Data = JSON.stringify(m);

      const p = $.post({ url: user.UserMethodUrl, data: ajaxObject }, (data) =>
      {
        const json = new JsonData();
        json.ParseEncodedData(data).then((data) =>
        {
          json.TrimAllKeysAndValues(data);

          let consigneeInfo = {};

          consigneeInfo.Company = data.shitem[0].Shsrce[0].Company;
          consigneeInfo.Contact = data.shitem[0].Shsrce[0].Contact;
          consigneeInfo.StreetAddress1 = data.StreetAddress1;
          consigneeInfo.StreetAddress2 = data.StreetAddress2;
          consigneeInfo.StreetAddress3 = data.StreetAddress3;
          consigneeInfo.City = data.shitem[0].Shsrce[0].City;
          consigneeInfo.State = data.shitem[0].Shsrce[0].State;
          consigneeInfo.PostalCode = data.shitem[0].Shsrce[0].Zip;
          consigneeInfo.Country = data.shitem[0].Shsrce[0].Country;

          //get the consignee information
          const lineItemProductInfo = data.shitem[0]; //Root : Item Number, Description, Ordered Count, etc

          console.log(consigneeInfo);
        })
      });
    })
  }

function ClientBusinessRules() {
    var vm;
    var loadselectedValue;

    this.PageLoaded = function(location) 
    {        
        vm = this.vm;
        if (location === '/shipping') {
            var aTags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
            var searchText = "Email";
            
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                for (var i = 0; i < aTags.length; i++) {
                    if (aTags[i].textContent == searchText) {
                        var loaded = aTags[i];
                        aTags[i].click();
                    }
                }
                
                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    pickupDeliveryPaneReady(pickupDeliveryPane);
                }
            }, 50); 
        }
        
           if (location === '/batchmanager') {
            $( "#btnCreateNewBatches" ).click(function() {                
                var userMethodParams = { "action": "CreateNewBatchForProcessing"};
            
                var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
            
                var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
            
            if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
                client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
            } 
            else {
                    alert("Batch creation request sent");
                }
            });
            
            $("#btnSetBatchAsPrinted").click(function() {

            var batchId = $('#cboAvailableBatchReferences').find(":selected").text();
            
            if(batchId !== null && batchId !== '')
            {
                var proceedToSetBatchPrinted = confirm("Confirm to set batch" + batchId + " as deleted? Click OK to continue or Cancel");
                
                if(proceedToSetBatchPrinted)
                {
                    var userMethodParams = { "action": "SetBatchAsPrinted", "batchid" : $('#cboAvailableBatchReferences').find(":selected").text()};
        
                    var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
        
                    var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
        
                    if (response.ErrorCode != 0) 
                    {
                        client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
                    } 
                    else 
                    {
                        alert(batchId + " was set to deleted");
                    }
                }
            }
            else
            {
                alert("No batch has been selected");
            }
            }); // end function
        }
    }

    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) 
    {               
        loadselectedValue=loadValue;
        // Converting JS object to an array
        shipmentRequestObject =  JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest));
        
        ChromeScrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);

        // Check for not found error
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(0,1) == '~')    
                {
                 alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(1));
				  $("input:text").eq(0).focus();   
			  this.vm.newShipment();
	        	return;
                }
        }
        
        //Send OSCO related errors to end user
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if (window.confirm(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20 + "\nContinue with shipment?")) 
            {
              //alert("You pressed OK");
            } 
            else 
            {
                $("input:text").eq(0).focus();
            }   
        }
      
        // Check for address validation required
        if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4 == 'Y')    
                {
                var interval = setInterval(function() {
                const consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                consigneeCompany = consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Company"]');
                consigneePostalCode = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="postalCode"]');
                consigneeCity = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                consigneeState = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');

                var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && consigneePostalCode.length && consigneeCity.length && consigneeState.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] button[title="Validate Address"]').click();                    
                    }
                }, 50);
            }
        }
  
        $('[name="address1"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1);
        
        $('[name="company"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company);
        
    //debugger;
    }
    
    function ChromeScrollIntoView(element, value) {
        if (!isIE()) {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                if (element.val() == value) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
     
                    var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                    var selectTop = element.offset().top;
     
                    element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                }
            }, 50);
        }
    }
     
    function isIE() {
        return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
    }

    $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]', 'change', function(e) {
        debugger
        var orderLoaded=loadselectedValue;
        var shipRequest=shipmentRequestObject;
        var address1=shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1;
        var loadedShipperValue = $('select[ng-change="vm.shipperChange()"]').val();
        var description;
        var returnsShipper = "STLRETURNS";
        var shipmentsShipper = "STLPKG";
        
            if (loadedShipperValue.substring(7) == returnsShipper) 
            {
                $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').val('SPEEDTECH.Custom.GND');
                DrawDataInReturnForm();
                MarkShipmentAsReturn();
                $('select[ng-change="vm.shipperChange()"]').prop('disabled', true);//disable the combobox after selecting STLRETURNS
            }
            
            if(loadedShipperValue.substring(7) == shipmentsShipper)
            {                
                $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]').prop("checked", false);                  
                $('[name="code"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Code);
                $('[name="company"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company);
                $('[name="contact"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Contact);
                $('[name="address1"]:eq(0)').val(address1);
                $('[name="address2"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address2);
                $('[name="address3"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address3);
                $('[name="city"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.City);
                $('[name="stateProvince"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince);
                $('[name="postalCode"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PostalCode);
                $('[name="Country"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country);
                $('[name="email"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);
                $('[name="phone"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Phone);
                $('[name="fax"]:eq(0)').val(shipRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Fax);
                $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').val('SPEEDTECH.Custom.GND');

                $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(orderLoaded);

                if(shipRequest.Packages[0] !='undefined')
                {
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]>option').prop('selected', false);
                    $('textarea[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val(shipRequest.Packages[0].Description);
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val(shipRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail);
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmailLocale"]').val(shipRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmailLocale);
                    UnMarkShipmentAsReturn();
                }
                $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference"]').val(orderLoaded);
            }      
    });

    function DrawDataInReturnForm(){
        var carrierEmailReturnLabelMethod = 5;
        $('form[name="returnForm"]').find('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val(RETURN_DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION);
        $('form[name="returnForm"]').find('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]').prop("checked", true);
        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]>option:eq('+ carrierEmailReturnLabelMethod +')').prop('selected', true);
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val(shipmentRequestObject.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);
    }

    function MarkShipmentAsReturn(){
        for (let i = 0; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++) 
        {
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDelivery = true;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = shipmentRequestObject.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Description = RETURN_DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION;             
        }
    }

    function UnMarkShipmentAsReturn(){
        for (let i = 0; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++) 
        {
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDelivery = false;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryMethod = undefined;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = '';
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Description = '';
        }
    }

    function ClearAllInputFields()
    {
        var loadedOrderValue = $('input[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').val();
        var elements = document.getElementsByTagName("input");        
        for (var ii=0; ii < elements.length; ii++) 
        {
            if (elements[ii].type == "text" && elements[ii].value != loadedOrderValue) 
            {
                elements[ii].value = "";
            }
        }  
        
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]').prop("checked", false);
        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]>option:eq(0)').prop('selected', true)
        $('textarea[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val();
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val();
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmailLocale"]').val();
         shipmentRequestObject =  {}
    }
    
    function thinClientAPIRequest (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON
    }
    
    var clientService = {
        config: $.getJSON({url:'config.json', async: false}).responseJSON,
        authorizationToken: function () {
            if (JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")))
                return { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token };
        }
    }
    
    var client = {
        userContext: function () {
            var userContextUrl = 'api/usercontext/GET';
            var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            if (shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http')) {
                var url = new URL(shipExecServiceUrl);
                userContextUrl = url.origin + '/' + userContextUrl;
            }
            var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
            return $.get({url: userContextUrl, headers: authorizationToken, async: false}).responseJSON;
        }(),
        dismiss: $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { $('div[role="alert"]:visible').hide(); }),
        alert: (function () {
            var closealert = $('<button class="close" />').append('<span>&times;</span>');
            var uibalert = $('<div hidden class="alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom ng-scope" role="alert" style="z-index: 2000;" />');
            uibalert.append(closealert).append('<span style="padding-right: 10px" />');

            $('body').append(uibalert);
            closealert.on('click', function () { uibalert.hide(); })

            return {
                Info: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-success alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-info').show();
                },
                Success: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
                },
                Danger: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-success');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
                }
            }
        })()
    }    
}

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {   
       debugger;
       if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress === undefined || shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress === null){
           if(!shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery){
              var userName = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.Contact;
              //alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper);
              var theShippers = this.vm.profile.Shippers;
              theShippers.forEach(shpr => {
                  if (shpr.Symbol === shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper) {
                      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {
                        Contact: userName,
                        Company: shpr.Company,
                        Address1: shpr.Address1,
                        Address2: shpr.Address2,
                        Address3: shpr.Address3,
                        City: shpr.City,
                        StateProvince: shpr.StateProvince,
                        PostalCode: shpr.PostalCode,
                        Country: shpr.Country,
                        Phone: shpr.Phone
                    };
                }
            });
          }
       }    
       
    };

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;
          var employeeID;
          var BU;
          var OU;
          var CR;
          var locationCode;
         var CustomData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
            for (var Custom in CustomData) {
                     if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom1") employeeID = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                      if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom2") BU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                       if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom3") OU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                        if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom4") CR = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                         if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom5")  locationCode= CustomData[Custom].Value;
             }
             
         if (CR === undefined || !isFiveDigitNumber(CR)) {
            alert('Invalid Cost Center');
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = employeeID;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = CR;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = CR;
         shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = BU;
          shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = locationCode;
    }

// Source: STAR INDIA CRAFT (STARINCRFT)_ISMEA_FTP_1583.cs
// function getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// function getUserContext() // returns void
function getUserContext() {
        debugger;
        if (userContext === undefined) {
            $.get({ url: "api/usercontext/GET", async:false })
            .done(function (data) {
               userContext = data;
            })
        }
    }

    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
    debugger;
    var consolidatedOpportunities = $("#txtConsolidatedFields").find('*').filter(':input:visible:first').val();
    
       if) ($("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked") && ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities))
       {
         var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("true",consolidatedOpportunities,loadValue);
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession;
       }
       else
       {
            var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("false","",loadValue);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession
       }
    }

// shipping() // returns void
function shipping() {
            vm.AddReturnLabel = function () {
            vm.currentShipment.Packages.push(getPackageObject());
            vm.totalPackages = vm.currentShipment.Packages.length;
            };

            vm.CreateReturnLabelFromPrevious = function () {
                debugger;
                vm.currentShipment = structuredClone(vm.lastShipmentRequest);
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery = true;
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
                vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.GND" };
                if (!vm.selectedServices) {
                    vm.selectedServices = [];
                }
                vm.selectedServices.push(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service);
            };
            

            function getPackageObject() {
                debugger;
                let addedPackage = structuredClone(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0]);
                addedPackage.ReturnDelivery = true;
                addedPackage.ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
                return addedPackage;
            };

        }

// getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// getUserContext() // returns void
function getUserContext() {
        debugger;
        if (userContext === undefined) {
            $.get({ url: "api/usercontext/GET", async:false })
            .done(function (data) {
               userContext = data;
            })
        }
    }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        console.log("SHIPPPING PAGE PRESHIP");
        console.log(this.vm);
        console.log(shipmentRequest);
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
        var ref1 = CheckReference(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference);
        var ref2 = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData) + "-" +
            CheckReference(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1);


        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = ref1;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ConsigneeReference = ref2;
        }

        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges == "consignee" || shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.DutiesAndCharges == "dutiesandcharges") {
            SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest);
        }
    };

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        console.log('new shipment');
        console.log(shipmentRequest);
         
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        var sf1 = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = sf1;

        if (typeof shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress !== "undefined") shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Code = "";
    };
