// this.PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreRate = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //console.log(this.vm);

        var yesText = "YES- Please ship Next Day Air";
        var noText = "";

        var shipNextDay = false;

        //Check to see if yes or no is selected = yes = next day air - no = gnd

        for (var t = 0; t < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; t++) {
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[t].ShipperReference == yesText) {
                shipNextDay = true;
                break;
            }

        }

        var selectedService = {};
        var allServices = false;
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.selectedServices.length; i++) {
            if (shipNextDay) {
                //Next day air
                if (this.vm.selectedServices[i].Symbol == "UPSAPI.UPS.NDA") {
                    selectedService = this.vm.selectedServices[i];
                    break;
                }
            } else {
                //ground
                if (this.vm.selectedServices[i].Symbol == "UPSAPI.UPS.GND") {
                    allServices = true;
                    break;
                    //selectedService = this.vm.selectedServices;   
                }
            }

        }
        if (allServices) {
            //create new variable to assign original list in post rate function
            this.vm.selectedServicesOriginalList = this.vm.selectedServices;
            this.vm.selectedServices = [];
            this.vm.selectedServices = this.vm.selectedServicesOriginalList;
        } else {
            //create new variable to assign original list in post rate function
            this.vm.selectedServicesOriginalList = this.vm.selectedServices;
            this.vm.selectedServices = [];
            this.vm.selectedServices.push(selectedService);
        }




        // console.log(shipNextDay);
        // console.log(this.vm);
    }

// this.PostRate(shipmentRequest, rateResults) // returns undefined
this.PostRate = function (shipmentRequest, rateResults) {
        this.vm.selectedServices = [];
        this.vm.selectedServices = this.vm.selectedServicesOriginalList;
    }

// Source: The Ohio State University (OSU)_OSU Reference Configuration Rule_89.cs
// PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;

        var shipToEmail = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);
        var shipFromEmail = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Email);
        var ref1 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1);
        var ref2 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2);
        var ref3 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
        var ref4 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4);
        var ref5 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5);
        var ref6 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6);
        var ref7 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7);
        var ref8 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8);

        var shipperRef = ref1 + "~" + ref2 + "~" + ref3 + "~" + ref4;
        var consigneeRef = ref5 + "~" + ref6;//ref7 + "~" + ref8 + "~" +

        shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg)
        {
            if(pkg.MiscReference7)
            {
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages.length > 1 ) {
                    throw ({message: 'Multiple Packages Not Support with Dry Ice', errorCode: ''});
                }

                if (returnPropertyValue(pkg.MiscReference8) === '')
                {
                    throw ({message: 'Missing Dry Ice Weight', errorCode: ''});
                }
                
                var ret = ref8;
                
                var DryIceWeight = {
                    "Amount": ret.replace('kgs',''),
                    "Units": "KG"
                };
				pkg.DryIceWeight = DryIceWeight;
				
				var Country = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country;
				console.log(Country);
				if(Country =="US"){
				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 1;
				}else{
				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 2;
				}
                pkg.DryIcePurpose = 2;
            }
            pkg.ShipperReference = shipperRef;
            pkg.ConsigneeReference = consigneeRef;
            pkg.MiscReference20 = userContext.UserId;

            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = '';
            pkg.ShipNotificationEmail = shipToEmail != '' || shipFromEmail != '';
            if (shipToEmail != '') {
                pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipToEmail;
            }

            if (shipFromEmail != '' ) {
                if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + shipFromEmail;
                } else {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipFromEmail;
                }
            }
        });
    }

        function getUserName() {
            debugger;
        var helloUser = $('a[title="Manage"]:contains("Hello")').text();
        return helloUser.match(/[a-zA-Z]+[a-zA-Z0-9._]+@[a-zA-Z]+\.[a-zA-Z.]{2,5}/i)[0];
    }

// DecodeReturnString(data) // returns parsed JSON object or undefined on error
    function DecodeReturnString(data){
	    try{
	        return JSON.parse($("<div />").html(data).text());
        }catch (error){
            console.log(error.name);
            console.log(error.message);
            console.log(data);
        }
    }

// DisplayLogoSaveMessage(result) // returns void
	function DisplayLogoSaveMessage(result) {

		var jsonLoad = jQuery.parseJSON(result);

		if (jsonLoad.logosuccess != null && jsonLoad.logosuccess != undefined) {

			if (jsonLoad.logosuccess != undefined) {
				alert(jsonLoad.logosuccess);
			}
			else {
				alert("There was an error attempting to save file to server.  File NOT updated, please try again.");
			}
		}
		else {

			if (jsonLoad != undefined && jsonLoad.error != null && jsonLoad.error != undefined) {
				alert(jsonLoad.error);
			}
			else {
				alert("There was an error attempting to save file to server.  File NOT updated, please try again.");
			}
		}
	}

// PageInitialize(viewModel) // returns undefined
this.PageInitialize = function(viewModel) {
        vm = viewModel;
        //console.log(client.userContext);
        var searchCriteria = {WhereClauses:[{ FieldName:"Name", FieldValue:"Company Address Book", Operator:0 }]};
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
        //var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, SearchCriteria: searchCriteria };
        
		//debugger;
		
        $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_Shared', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
        {
            //console.log('response from inside method: ', response);

            if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
            {
                var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;
    
                data = { UserContext: client.userContext, AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
                //console.log(data);
                
                $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
                {
                    //console.log(response);
                    if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
                    {
                        tpbAddressBookEntries = response.AddressBookEntries;
                        vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes = tpbAddressBookEntries;
                    }                    
                    //debugger;
                }));
            }
        }));

    };

// Source: VSP (VSP)_VSP Reference Rules_81.cs
// PageInitialize(viewModel) // returns undefined
    this.PageInitialize = function(viewModel) {
        vm = viewModel;
        //console.log(client.userContext);
        var searchCriteria = {WhereClauses:[{ FieldName:"Name", FieldValue:"Company Address Book", Operator:0 }]};
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
        //var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, SearchCriteria: searchCriteria };
        
		debugger;
		
        $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
        {
            //console.log('response from inside method: ', response);

            if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
            {
                var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;
    
                data = { UserContext: client.userContext, AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
                //console.log(data);
                
                $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
                {
                    //console.log(response);
                    if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
                    {
                        tpbAddressBookEntries = response.AddressBookEntries;
                        vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes = tpbAddressBookEntries;
                    }                    
                    debugger;
                }));
            }
        }));

    };

// thinClientAPIRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns jqXHR from $.post
        thinClientAPIRequest: function (method, data, isAsync) {
            var shipExecServiceUrl = client.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            var authorizationToken = client.getAuthorizationToken();
			debugger;
            return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken });
        },

// Source: WOODLAND MFG (WLMI)_WoodLand_CBR_1644.cs
// GetWeight() // returns void
    this.GetWeight = function () {
        if (this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration !== null) {
           
            var url = "https://localhost:5001/api/Scale/Read";
            var data ={
                "PortType": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.PortType,
                "Port": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.Port,
                "UsbVid": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.UsbVid,
                "UsbPid": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.UsbPid,
                "RequestCommand": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RequestCommand,
                "StopBits": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.StopBits,
                "Parity": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Parity,
                "RequestTimeout": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RequestTimeout,
                "HostAddress": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.HostAddress,
                "RegexPattern": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RegexPattern,
                "DeviceParser": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.DeviceParserType,
                "DeviceName": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Name,
                "Handshake": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Handshake
            };
            var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: data, async: false }).responseJSON;
            //debugger;
            console.log(data);
            console.log(ret);
            
            if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                
                this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].Weight = {
                    "Amount": ret.Weight,
                    "Units": "LB"
                };
               
                if (ret.HasDimensions) {
                    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].Dimensions = {
                        "Length": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[0],
                        "Width": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[1],
                        "Height": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[2],
                        //"Units": ret.DimensionUnit.toUpperCase() === "IN" ? 0 : 1
                        "Units": "In"
                    };
                }
            }
        }
    };

// Source: Worldwide Cargo Services Inc (WORLDWIDECSI)_API TEST_1781.cs
// PostalCodeLookup(addressName) // returns void
    this.PostalCodeLookup = function (addressName) {
debugger;
        var userContext = this.getUserContext(this);
        var postalCode = $('[address-property-name="' + addressName + '"] [name="postalCode"]').val();
        var content = { AddressName: addressName, PostalCode: postalCode };
        var payload = { Action: 'CSZ', Content: JSON.stringify(content) };
        var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(payload), UserContext: userContext };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).responseJSON;
        if (response.ErrorCode > 0) {
            client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', response.ErrorMessage)
        } else {
            var responseData = JSON.parse(client.htmlText(response.Data));        
            if (responseData == null) {
                client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', 'Invalid or Not US Postal Code');
            } else {
                if (responseData.length > 1) {
                    this.addressResults = responseData;
                    client.shipping.validateAddressModalShow();
                } else {
                    this.currentShipment.updateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, responseData[0].City, responseData[0].StateProvince)
                }
            }
        }
    }

// CreateShipmentAutoSubmit(keyEvent) // returns void
    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {
        if (keyEvent.keyCode === 13 || keyEvent.keyCode === 9) {            
            event.preventDefault();
debugger;
            var $createShipmentBtn = $('#createShipmentBtn');
            var createShipmentInput = '#buildShipmentModalBody input';

            if (document.activeElement.id == $createShipmentBtn.attr('id')) {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // click on create build button if sending tab or enter while focus is on button
                    $createShipmentBtn.click();
                }
            } else {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // allow shipper chance to change weight unit
                    $createShipmentBtn.focus();
                }
            }
        }

        function isInputsEmpty($inputs) {
            var inputsIsEmpty = false;
            $inputs.each(function () {
                if (this.type == 'text') {
                    if (this.value.trim() == "") {
                        this.focus();
                        inputsIsEmpty = true;
                        return false;
                    };
                };
            });
            return inputsIsEmpty;
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        vm = this.vm;
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;
        shipmentRequest.CreateShipmentSubmit = this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit;
        shipmentRequest.CreateShipment = this.BuildShipment;

        // debugger;
    }
